Important Foreign News

Japanese Militarists Advocate Armed Aggression Against China

Advocating Increasing Troops in Manchuria and Mongolia to Protect Interests

Issuing a General Order to All Military Attaches in China to Pay Attention to Our Country's Actions

▲ Tokyo News, Since the Minister of the Army, Minami, convened a meeting of division commanders on the 4th of this month, arguments for expanding the military and defending interests in Manchuria and Mongolia by force have stimulated public sentiment. Various troops, local veterans associations, youth leagues, and various nationalist organizations throughout the country have echoed and supported them. The rise of this kind of public opinion is actually due to the military's planned propaganda and advocacy, and the ignorant masses who are obsessed with aggressive militarism have responded to the militarists' advocacy. The impact of this military movement on politics and diplomacy is not insignificant. At the meeting of division commanders, Minister Minami strongly criticized the government authorities and Shidehara diplomacy, saying that those people were outsiders who were not qualified to discuss military affairs. He strongly advocated defending interests in Manchuria and Mongolia by force, so that they could develop. He also said, "The current situation in Manchuria and Mongolia is actually due to the long-term cultivation of exclusionary national sovereignty recovery thinking by the neighboring country, and the development of new economic power, which is by no means a temporary phenomenon, but will be a continuous situation." Recently, all the military attaches of Japanese consulates in various parts of China have been replaced. Minister Minami issued a general order to the newly appointed military attaches stationed in various places to pay close attention to the movements of China. The most noteworthy of these is the argument for increasing troops in Manchuria and Mongolia. As for the details of the plan, it is difficult to obtain. Minister Minami's advocacy of a hegemonic policy towards China, with increasing troops in Manchuria and Mongolia as the top priority, shows that the Japanese militarists' plan for armed aggression against our country is becoming more active. Minister Minami is the most enthusiastic leader, and the people of the country should pay attention to it. (World News Agency)

League of Nations Drafts Plan to Develop China's Industry

▲ Geneva News on the 17th of the National Society, The International Labour Office established by the League of Nations announced today that the bureau is currently drafting a ten-year construction plan for China, the content of which is modeled on the Soviet Union's five-year plan and will be carried out in five aspects: (1) Reclaiming 300 million mu of wasteland, (2) Developing transportation and communications, (3) Building seaports, (4) Building 8 million tons of merchant ships, the third and fourth items are related, (5) Building factories across the country to revitalize industry, this plan will be half-implemented by the National Government and half-implemented by government-controlled companies, it is estimated that the total implementation will require the purchase of 12 million tons of steel and 200 million tons of coal, and the horsepower required by the factories will also reach 20 million. According to people in the Labour Office, this plan has been approved by the National Government in general, but it has not been mentioned how the funds will be raised. (According to the weekly magazine issued by the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Visiting Bureau of the Ministry of Industry on May 23, there is also a record of the National Government's publication of the ten-year construction plan.)

Important French Statements Amidst the Implementation of the Hoover Plan

Declaring Unwillingness to Give Up Reparations and Amend the Treaty of Versailles

International Bankers Meet to Agree to Extend German Short-Term Loans for Six Months

President of the Bank of England Goes to Canada, Seven More American Banks Close

▲ Paris News on the 17th of the National Society, French Finance Minister Flandin stated to the press today that France will never give up its due reparations, and denounced the absurdity of saying that the world's economic downturn is due to the payment of war debts. He said that if the theory that the economy could be revived after the cancellation of war debts was credible, then the neutral countries during the European war did not have the burden of war debts, and today they are also experiencing economic decline, and there are now several countries that do not bear war debts, and their economic situation is as serious as that of Germany. Therefore, France does not want to receive one less penny of the reparations that Germany should pay, and does not allow the modification of debt and the Treaty of Versailles.

▲ Basel News on the 17th of Reuters, The talks among international bankers here have not yet yielded an agreement. The biggest difficulty is what method to use to make Germany's existing foreign debt flow without hindering the German currency. Another dispatch said that international bankers have completed their work tonight and passed the report of the British representative Leighton, extending the short-term loans to Germany of about 5 billion marks for six months, but this case is subject to conditions, and it must wait until the central banks of Britain and the United States are prepared to extend their loans for six months from August 18 before it takes effect. Furthermore, the Bank for International Settlements, which has approved a loan of 1 billion marks to Germany, must also agree, and this case is scheduled to be signed tomorrow.

▲ Basel News on the 18th of Reuters, The British representative's report also advocates lending new funds to Germany under certain conditions. International bankers have agreed on a way to prevent foreign countries from continuing to withdraw funds from Germany. The issue of extending the mark loans has not yet been resolved. Most of the members have left here, while the two German representatives are still staying, hoping to reach an agreement on the mark loans at the last minute this morning by making a phone call to Berlin.

▲ New York News on the 18th of Reuters, Wall Street is very excited about the President of the Bank of England, Norman, going to Canada. It should be complied with, in addition to drafting practical measures with the Ministry of Interior for submission. Considering the urgency of raising relief funds, it is proposed to issue 10 million yuan of disaster relief public bonds in the twentieth year of the Republic of China, to be issued in September of this year, so that they can be distributed to the disaster areas, and the starving people can receive substantial benefits as soon as possible. Is this appropriate? A draft of the public bond regulations and the principal and interest repayment schedule are submitted for review and forwarded to the National Government for submission to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation and promulgation. Resolution: Forwarded to the National Government for submission to the Legislative Yuan. Yan Moves to White Buddha Hall

▲ Will Return to Dalian Soon

▲ Preparations Underway for Exchange between Shang and Xu

Taiyuan Dispatch: Since the defeat at Shibu and the stabilization of the overall situation, there have been many rumors regarding the Shanxi situation due to Yan's return to Shanxi. When Yan first returned, all parties paid close attention, saying that he would cooperate with someone or compromise with someone. Therefore, although Yan repeatedly stated that he was purely returning to his hometown to visit relatives, the society did not believe it. Recently, the atmosphere of so-called compromise and cooperation with someone has gradually disappeared. Yan, when visiting generals, besides advising them to implement unity, rarely expressed other opinions. In the past two or three days, his attitude has become increasingly passive, and he has closed his doors to guests, appearing helpless. A person from the riverside recently said that when Yan first returned, many people went to visit him upon hearing the news, and it was very lively. Yan was also very interested in the reunion after a long separation. Recently, too many visitors have come, in order to avoid harassment and to avoid misunderstandings caused by private socializing, he moved the day before yesterday to the White Buddha Hall in the depths of the mountains more than thirty miles away from the Dingxiang County, and temporarily recuperated. All visitors are uniformly rejected, and several adjutants are sent to stay at the Dingxiang County bus station, where they politely decline visitors halfway and prevent them from going. It is said that Yan plans to return to Dalian in the near future. Judging from the current situation, the future of Shanxi will definitely not be improved by Yan's return. As for the change of chairman, after Xu Yongchang was officially decided by the National Government, all departments of the provincial government are actively preparing for the handover. The members went to Xu's residence yesterday morning to urge him to take office. Secretary-General Li Jingrong also personally went to visit him and asked him to take office as soon as possible so that someone could be responsible for the provincial administration. Xu said that he still had to rush to Pingyi for a trip and ask Deputy Commander Zhang for instructions before he could make a decision, and instructed Li to maintain the status quo temporarily. After Li returned to the government, he immediately convened a temporary meeting of section chiefs to discuss the handover. It is reported that Xu has informally expressed his future administrative policy, saying that on the active side, he plans to first suppress bandits to stabilize the people's hearts, eliminate poisons to eliminate the people's harm, and strictly organize the provincial government and various departments, so that the foundation can be consolidated and jointly responsible for overcoming this difficult time. (August 14)

▲ Xu Tingyao Ordered to Resolve Liu's Troops

▲ Liu Guitang Leads Troops to Hide in the City of Daming

Liu Guitang originally had a unit stationed outside the city of Daming and a unit stationed inside the city of Daming. The unit stationed outside the city, about a thousand cavalrymen, was surrounded and disarmed by Xu's division five days ago. However, Liu Guitang himself led two infantry regiments, about four thousand men, and retreated into the city of Daming, refusing to come out. Liu recently sent a telegram to Jinan to Han Fuqu, asking him to intercede with the central government. Han believed that resolving the troops was a central government order, and that the troops were composed of bandits, so it was not convenient to interfere, and he ignored it. Today (August 16) afternoon, according to Jiang Bocheng, regarding the resolution of Liu Guitang's troops, the central government ordered the Fourth Division to be responsible for handling it. A part of Liu's troops has been resolved, and the rest have retreated into the city of Daming. The central government has sent a telegram to Jinan, ordering Chairman Han to send troops to assist in resolving Liu's troops. Li's brigade stationed in Dezhou and the unit stationed in Enxian immediately mobilized, taking the road through Xiajin and Weixian to ambush Daming. Li Xuande's cavalry brigade stationed in Guantao also moved to intercept. (August 16)

Macau Armory Explosion

▲ All Lights in Macau Extinguished

▲ Many Houses Collapsed

▲ Sixty to Seventy People Killed or Injured

▲ Losses Estimated at Over 300,000

Macau Dispatch: There were originally three Portuguese armories in Macau, one under the Guia Lighthouse, one in Coloane, and one in the harbor. Among them, the armory under the Guia Lighthouse stored a lot of bullets and explosives. Suddenly, at about 5:40 a.m. on the 13th, for unknown reasons, it suddenly exploded. The sound of the explosion was loud and far away, and the shock was extremely strong. The residents on land and water were awakened by it. At the same time, the electric lights were also destroyed by the shock, resulting in a dark world. Moreover, Macau was covered in thick smoke, and it was almost suspected that something had happened in Macau. After the residents woke up, they felt the walls shaking and about to collapse, and many ran to the streets to escape, their cries shaking the sky, which was unbearable to hear. At that time, the ships at sea were moved by the shock, as if in huge waves. Even large ships such as the Quanzhou steamer were shaking. At the same time, the Macau government issued an unexpected alarm, and the residents suspected that it was a military disaster. The embarrassing situation can be imagined. It is reported that when the incident occurred, all of the new houses of the Li family on the Erlonghou Road near the armory, more than ten in total, had several doors and walls collapsed, and some had collapsed completely, resulting in the death of many people. Later, the fire brigade sent a large number of personnel in vehicles and equipment to the rescue. The police station, in addition to sending a large number of Chinese and Western detectives to the scene to maintain order, also telegraphed to various districts to send additional police to the scene to assist in the rescue. However, still afraid that it was not enough, more than a hundred soldiers and black soldiers were transferred, carrying iron shovels to the scene to assist in the excavation. The engineer's office also sent engineers to the scene to help. The dead and wounded who were dug out were sent by car to the National Hospital on the hilltop, the White Horse Hospital, and the Kiang Wu Hospital for treatment. The excavation continued until about 12:00 noon before the team returned. It is reported that the number of deaths and injuries is about sixty to seventy. More than ten black soldiers guarding the armory and one clerk were unable to escape and were killed on the spot. As for the new houses of the Li family on Erlonghou Road, the Chinese and Western residents suffered the most injuries. The most tragic of them was the residence of Jian Huanzhang, the former Supervisor of Linhuai Customs and the current Director of the Finance Bureau of Zhongshan County, at No. 37. Jian Huanzhang, his wife Ms. Ma, and his brother Jian Zuan were killed on the spot. Only one person escaped. The corpses of Jian Huanzhang and others have been carried to the hospital for collection by coolies. Zheng Peisheng, a ticket seller for the Qiguan bus, was injured in the head by a flying stone when he passed by the car factory early in the morning to return to work and died on the spot. Huang Jiu, a driver at No. 92 Koka Road, was still in bed when a large stone flew from the tile surface and broke the roof beam, injuring Huang Jiu's hand and mouth on the spot. His wife was also slightly injured. The Jin Yi firecracker shop in Shakang was also hit by stones and the tile surface was smashed. Partner Li Guang was injured in both feet, and his friend Li He was also injured in the head. The Cantonese opera troupe Jue Xiansheng was performing on the Longtian stage and the show had just ended ten minutes before the explosion when a large stone flew to the door outside the courtyard and destroyed a prop box. The tile surface of the stage was also lifted, and mud and tiles flew everywhere. One actor was hit in the head by a tile. The houses near Guia were mostly cracked by the shock, and many Portuguese women and children were injured by tiles and stones. There were also many injured in other streets, and the police detectives are continuously investigating in various hospitals. More than 50% of the glass windows in the streets of the Guia area were shattered, so the streets and lanes were full of glass. Fortunately, the firecracker and gunpowder armory was not affected, otherwise the disaster would have been even worse. As for the wealthy people living on the hillside of Guia, several of them had many treasured antiques, which were also shaken and fell to the ground, resulting in a large number of broken pieces. Therefore, the total loss in Macau is estimated to be around 300,000 yuan. (August 14)

The Saying of the Opening of the Gold Mine in the Xing'an District

▲ Exploring Gold Veins Now, Not Talking About Mining

▲ The Saying of Ten Years of British Patent Is Completely Absurd

▲ Zou Zuohua Returns Home Via America After Visiting Austria and England

Tianjin Dispatch: Recently, various newspapers in Beiping, Tianjin, and Shanghai have repeatedly published news about the opening of gold mines in North Manchuria and the Xing'an District, and the granting of ten-year and twenty-year British patents. This matter is of great importance to China's mining rights. The reporter specially sent a letter to Gao Renfu, the Tuntian General Office of the Xing'an District (Note: Tuntian Supervisor Zou Zuohua was ordered to go to Europe and the United States to inspect reclamation affairs, and went abroad in May of this year. Gao is acting as the supervisor). After receiving a reply, it is known that someone is spreading rumors. The main points are excerpted as follows, which I think will be welcomed by those who care about mining sovereignty: "I have received your letter and thank you for your instructions. Although the gold mines in our district are rich in reserves, we have not gone through the exploration procedures, so we do not know the quality. This exploration personnel is extremely lacking in the country. Therefore, when our supervisor went abroad, he made an agreement with a gold mining company to conduct exploration on his behalf. It is purely for exploration purposes and does not involve mining or patents. The contract is based on this intention. Unexpectedly, the opponents would abandon the facts, pick up floating words, and attack each other. This is very unfounded. However, such things are not uncommon. Our office has always adhered to the principle of ignoring them. If someone inquires, please explain the facts on our behalf. Right and wrong have their own public opinion, and those who bark at shadows cannot confuse the facts. Our supervisor is currently traveling from Austria to England. After he transfers to the Americas for inspection, he will seek to return."

When Zou Zuohua passed through Tianjin to go abroad this summer, he told reporters that the gold mines in the Xing'an District were very rich in reserves. Although they had been surveyed once, it was difficult to be sure of the total amount of gold veins. This trip plans to recruit experienced mining engineers from Europe and the United States for further detailed exploration. Our country's monetary system is based on silver. At this time of high gold prices, our country's foreign debts and international trade suffer great losses. Our country's red gold has always been used as women's ornaments, and the amount is limited. After the gold price rises, it is purchased and flows into foreign countries. If the gold standard is changed, silver must be used to purchase gold from foreign countries. This loss is even greater. Our country has no such power. Therefore, I strongly advocate opening more gold mines. If the gold mines in the Xing'an District are rich, the mining is proper, and it becomes the source of our country's recoining gold coins, it is also an expected thing. However, it is difficult to achieve great results without strong capital to mine gold mines. The financial resources of the Northeast are limited, and in the future, we hope that domestic wealthy businessmen will invest. During my trip abroad, I passed through Nanyang. In addition to promoting investment in reclamation in the Northeast to overseas Chinese, I also awakened their attention to mining gold mines. Because the overseas Chinese have huge capital and love the motherland, they are willing to invest in domestic production. As for the use of foreign capital to run industries, it is the proposition of the late Prime Minister Sun Yat-sen, but loans should be based on the principle of not damaging sovereignty. However, this matter depends on the future situation. The Northeast is very rich in resources and is coveted by Japan and Russia, who are fighting to seize it. If I do not plan for myself, others will plan for me. I hope that the people of the Northeast and the national experts will pay special attention. From this, it can be proved where the rumor of allowing British patents for ten years originated. (August 15)

The Excavation of Qian Wencan's Remains

▲ Only Obtained Bayonets and Clothing, Etc.

Jinan Dispatch: The excavation of Qian Wencan's remains has been recorded in previous news. In addition, there were many soda bottles,洋鐵罐, and other items. Although bones have not yet been unearthed, only Qian was harmed at Donglu School at that time. Japanese clothes did not need to be burned at that time. It seems that the clothes belong to Qian. However, the pit where they were burned is six or seven feet long and two or three feet deep. The bones of one person are limited, and it is not easy to find them after burning. This afternoon, they are still continuing the excavation. There is a well in the school, which is waterless and more than thirty feet deep. After the May 3rd Incident, the well was filled. Today, the well is being excavated together, and it has been excavated to more than ten feet deep. According to Ms. Yu Peiyuan, Qian's wife, her late husband not only died for the public, but was also brutally killed by foreigners. This matter concerns national humiliation. Whether or not the remains are obtained is not certain, but all human efforts have been exhausted. The May 3rd Memorial Committee here hosted Qian's wife and others yesterday. The Water Level of the Canal and the Current Situation of Dike Protection

▲ Li Mingyang Reports After Inspection

▲ Huai'an and Gaoyou Canal Water Gradually Recedes

Li Mingyang, the commissioner of the Su Province Committee and concurrent security commissioner, went to northern Jiangsu a few days ago to supervise the people of various counties along the canal to protect the dikes. He returned to the province yesterday. According to him, the water level of the canal and the dike protection situation are roughly as follows: Last Sunday (August 11), I was entrusted by the committee and departed for northern Jiangsu on the 12th to inspect the flood and supervise the protection of the dikes. First, I arrived at Yangzi Bridge. The water level was still gentle, but the water height would be level with the dike. Then I arrived at the Shaobo area. The water level was quite dangerous and had risen above the old dike. After continuously adding sand and soil and driving piles to protect it, the project was still good. If the west wind does not rise, it may not overflow. Later, I arrived at Cheluoba and saw that the water level was fierce, like the rushing of sea waves. When I went up to Gaoyou, I received a telephone report in the evening that there was a danger in Huaichengwan. I immediately ordered the rescue first and rushed to the site early on the 13th. I saw that the dike work there was all piled up with sand and mud, which was inevitably easy to collapse. Therefore, the top of the dike was still good, but the back had already collapsed first. Therefore, about one mile of the dike in that place was washed down by the wind and waves by two feet. Later, a crack was found, but it had been protected with sandbags and driving piles, and the work of widening the dike was underway. Twenty miles further up from there, passing through Longwang Temple, all the way to Binying, the dike was very dangerous. When I went there with the workers, I immediately built a dike there to save the emergency. This section of the dike work was all blocked with reeds and willow branches to slow down the water flow and reduce the risk of the dike being washed by the waves. The project above Baoying is considered to be the best in Huai'an, because the local area has a very strict organization, carefully planned measures, and township chiefs supervise the prevention, so the work is very strong. Now, although the water is rising, the river dikes are two and a half or three feet above the water surface. Going up to Qingjiang again, I arrived early on the 14th and went to the first and second gates. I saw that the water had entered several inches, and the banks around the upstream had already overflowed, relying entirely on Pu Ma bags to defend against the water. The water volume of the second gate and the first gate differed by several feet, and there were several leaks. Because the upstream water volume was very large, this place was a bit narrow and it was not easy to discharge, so it was even more critical. As for the prevention methods, all places used sandbags to fill in. The situation was really very dangerous. Whether it was safe or not was still a question. As for the houses on the shore, according to what I saw, some were flooded with only a roof left. The people moved to the river dikes and built tents to live in. When the water rose, they dug soil and drove piles to fill in. If they were washed down, they would go into the sea with the water. The tragic situation was unbearable to imagine. The flood situation this time was really extremely serious. Every time I set off for a county, I gathered people for training and ordered them to be responsible for the protection and to follow the Water Conservancy Bureau's plan. The required manpower should be fully recruited, otherwise, only the county heads of each county would be held accountable. Today, I returned to the province with Director Mao to report to the committee. I still have to go to supervise the dike protection.

The Huaiyi sources of the canal in Jiangsu Province have seen a slight decline. It is known that the Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau received a deleted telegram from Provincial Committee Wang Jingtao, Chief Engineer of the Water Conservancy Bureau Pei Yixiang, and others, which briefly stated that Huai'an was sunny and windless yesterday afternoon and this morning, and the water had fallen four inches. In addition, the Gaoyou Works reported in a telegram that the water at Yumatou on the 16th had fallen one inch, with a water storage of one zhang nine feet five inches. Huai'an and Gaoyou are located in the middle of the canal. Since the water has receded in both the upper and lower reaches, it is a good sign. It is hoped that the weather will be sunny for a long time and that the west wind will not rise, so that the excessive water can be discharged smoothly. It is also heard that Director Mao returned to the province from Qingjiang yesterday to visit Director Sun and reported on the river defense affairs. He will return to work this morning.

Minutes of the Second Jiangsu Provincial Congress of Representatives

▲ First General Assembly on the Morning of the 18th

▲ Two Important Proposals Passed According to the Agenda

▲ Provincial Government Commissioners Report in the Afternoon

Yesterday (the 18th) was the fourth day of the Second Jiangsu Provincial Congress of Representatives. The first formal meeting was held at 9:30 AM. The presidium publicly elected Zhang Minquan as chairman. Eighty-seven representatives attended. After the usual formalities, a work report from the Provincial Party Rectification Committee was given. In addition to a thick written copy, Representative Zhang Yuanyang was assigned to explain, stating that the Provincial Party Rectification Committee was ordered to be organized on December 11th of the 18th year (of the Republic), and it has been nearly two years since then. All the work has been compiled into a book, requesting all representatives to carefully examine and correct it, so that the new executive and supervisory committees can learn from it in the future. The two years of work can be divided into three periods. The first period was from its establishment on December 18th of the 18th year to July 31st of the 19th year. At that time, the strength of the party was weak, and the environment was dangerous. The rectification began by rectifying the thoughts and actions of all comrades in the province, with the sole goal of supporting the central government and implementing anti-communism, paying attention to the publicity of the party's correct theories, issuing the "Party Affairs Weekly," and organizing mobile propaganda teams. This was the important work of the first period. The second period was from August 1st of the 19th year to December 31st of the 19th year, focusing on practical work, dealing with matters and not people, first conducting a general survey of party affairs, enriching the internal work of each county, restricting the leave or concurrent positions of committee members and staff, unifying the finances of each county, and then providing district guidance to organize people's organizations, achieving the effect of party-government cooperation. Party districts were also divided, and a work outline and implementation plan for party members were formulated, and the Su-Xu party newspapers were handled. This was the second period. The third period was from January of the 20th year to the present, reorganizing and completing according to the central government's new organization, unifying authority and facilitating work. The party affairs of each county have also achieved great results. The important work was to handle the election of the National Assembly and establish official party headquarters in more than 50 counties, and to prepare for this provincial congress of representatives. In short, the past Provincial Party Rectification Committee has been working according to the law in everything, hoping that in addition to the representatives correcting it, they can properly discuss a plan for the new executive and supervisory committee, so that Jiangsu party affairs will never need to be rectified again in the future. After the report, the Huai'an representative raised questions, requesting Zhang Yuanyang to answer. Then Xu Wenjun stood up and spoke, saying that for the sake of saving time, the questioning representatives should submit their questions in writing to the Provincial Party Rectification Committee for answers. More than twenty people spoke one after another, with proponents and opponents debating for a long time. Chairman Zhang Minquan's voice was quite low, and he could not summarize the representatives' words in the midst of the chaos. Then a certain representative stood up and criticized Zhang, demanding that someone with a correct and loud pronunciation be replaced as chairman. The presidium had no choice but to announce a five-minute break, which brought a little calm. Then Yang Xingqin came out to be the chairman, offering opinions on the questioning matters, first proposing the establishment of an organizational work report review committee, and designating Shen Youguang and Huang Hansheng as reviewers, which was rejected by the public. Then he proposed that when a representative had questions about the work report, they should submit them in writing to the presidium, and submit them to the next meeting, requesting the representatives of the Provincial Party Rectification Committee to answer. This was passed by the majority of representatives. Next, Xu Wenjun, the representative of the proposal review committee, reported that the congress had received many proposals, and the review committee decided to divide them into nine categories: party affairs, administration, finance, education, construction, industry, justice, public security, and others. Each category was reviewed by a committee member, and each item was mimeographed and distributed. After the report, the proposals were discussed: (1) A case to send a telegram of condolence to the soldiers suppressing the bandits (proposed by the Provincial Party Rectification Committee) was passed unanimously without objection. (2) A case to send a telegram of condolence to the overseas Chinese who were victims in Korea, and to request the central government to seriously negotiate the Wanbaoshan incident and the Korean case (proposed by the Provincial Party Rectification Committee) was passed unanimously without objection. (3) The flood in this province is extremely severe, and methods should be urgently sought to provide relief. The representatives contributed many opinions on the outline of the fundamental and symptomatic treatments. It was past noon, and the chairman announced the adjournment.

At 2 PM in the afternoon, the general assembly continued. The agenda was the work reports of the various agencies of the provincial government. Before the meeting began, the entrance of Baoxian Park was filled with cars, as all the department heads below Chairman Ye of the provincial government arrived one after another. Written reports of the work of each agency had already been submitted to the congress. In order to prepare for questions, they all came to the meeting place in person to answer. After the meeting, the presidium elected Ge Jianshi as chairman, and after leading the ceremony, Chairman Ye Chucang of the provincial government first reported, briefly stating that since the establishment of the current provincial government, there has been no barrier between the provincial government and the various departments. He himself also considered himself a responsible chairman, but he felt that it was wrong that he had not been able to make significant achievements in the governance of Jiangsu Province. In this year, the provincial government properly formulated methods for employing people and suppressing bandits. Due to the economic panic, he felt that it was very difficult to provide relief for the current water shortage. After the report, Representative Wang Guoying spoke, hoping that the provincial government would strictly enforce rewards and punishments in the future. Luo Mingya hoped to pay attention to practical local issues. Next, Hu Pu'an, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, reported, with four main points: (1) the appointment of county magistrates, (2) the appointment of district chiefs, (3) the situation of water and land public security, and (4) disaster relief measures. The statement on the appointment of county magistrates lasted for a long time, exceeding the prescribed twenty minutes, so the chairman rang the bell to stop it. Tang Xincheng, the representative of Taixian County, Ma Wenzao of Suqian, Liu Chengrui and Qiu Youzhen of Tongshan all stated the illegal situations of the former or current county magistrates of their respective counties, and Hu agreed to answer them in person. Next, Xu Baoying, the director of the Department of Finance, reported his main points: (1) Since the 19th year, the revenue and expenditure of Jiangsu Province has been about 24 million yuan, but the revenue is very small and the debt is very large. The 20th year is even more difficult, with less revenue and more expenditure. (2) The adjustment of land tax is planned to start with land survey. (3) Eliminate the accumulated abuses of grain books, but without the fish scale register, it is very difficult to do it for a while. (4) The business tax has not achieved much since last year, and the amount collected is still far from the budget. (5) There is a public debt official debt of 7 million, with more than 5 million still owed for construction of 7 million. Jiangsu has always been known as a wealthy area, but in the 20th year, it has reached the point of exhaustion, and the reason is internal turmoil, the Communist Party, and this year's flood. However, he himself is extremely willing to do it with a spirit of great fearlessness. After the report, Representative Liu Youkang raised questions about the surcharges, grain transport, and grain book handling fees. Cai Peifu questioned the Jiangyin Finance Bureau about the deficit in education funds. Hu Chongji requested that the financial bureaus of each county not divert useful funds for other purposes. Next, Chen Hexian, the director of the Department of Education, reported in detail on higher, primary, secondary, and social education, as well as education funds, with the general idea of making young students stable in their studies. After the report, representatives Dai Zhiqiang, Xie Chengyu, and others asked many questions, and Chen agreed to answer them in detail in writing. Next, Sun Hongzhe, the director of the Department of Construction, reported, first describing the changes in the organizational structure of construction administration in the province, and then requesting this year's Grand Canal disaster.

▲ The Hangzhou City Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Industry yesterday, saying that the association has been established for one year and the second congress of members will be held on September 18th. A special request was made to the ministry to issue a seal.

▲ Zhou Yansun, the magistrate of Chongde County, has submitted his resignation due to the shortfalls in land tax collection. The provincial government has reassigned Mao Gaokun to take over.

▲ The Ministry of Industry ordered the Zhejiang Construction Department to investigate the major handicrafts in Zhejiang Province and report the findings. The Construction Department has already issued an order to the governments of all counties and cities to comply.

▲ Zhang Nanxian, the chairman of the provincial government, received a letter from the Hubei Provincial Association requesting assistance with disaster relief. Zhang specially convened colleagues from Hubei to discuss and decided that those with salaries above 200 yuan should donate 30 percent, those above 100 yuan to 200 yuan should donate 20 percent, those from 100 yuan to 50 yuan should donate 10 percent, and those below 50 yuan should donate according to their ability.

▲ The Construction Department's plan to renovate the Ou River was previously ordered by the Water Conservancy Bureau to organize a survey team. According to the current report, the start-up cost is more than 4,000 yuan, and the monthly recurring cost is about 2,000 yuan. The department decided that it was unable to allocate funds due to the shortage of provincial coffers. It was decided to wait until the Fifth District Water Conservancy Conference was established, and then order a deliberation and report.

▲ The Hangzhou City Chamber of Commerce issued a circular to the guilds of various industries. According to the order of the municipal government, commercial registration will begin on September 1st. Those who have previously received industrial and commercial registration certificates from the municipal government shall handle the matter in accordance with Article 34 of the Provisional Rules for Commercial Registration.

The identities of the bandits were verified in court, and they were tied to Fengaotang and shot to death to show the public.

Suzhou

Principals of primary schools petition against budget cuts. The educational circles of Wu County are dissatisfied with the Education Bureau's austerity policy, and a major dispute has occurred. The Education Association submitted a presentation to the Education Department yesterday (the 18th), requesting that someone be sent to thoroughly investigate to clarify the truth. The principals of the primary schools in the county sent representatives Zhang Ziming, etc., to the Education Bureau yesterday (the 18th) to petition, but there were no concrete results. Methods for raising construction bonds. The Wu County Government and Finance Bureau have repeatedly received orders from the department, limited to raising 200,000 yuan of construction bonds before the 30th of this month. The heads of the county bureau are quite hesitant about this matter. The chairman of the Chamber of Commerce and the members of the bond raising committee have consulted once. The members believe that at this time of popular poverty and financial exhaustion, how can such a huge amount of debt be raised? It is proposed to purchase several tens of thousands from the more than 100,000 yuan of construction special funds accumulated in Wu County to meet the urgent need. The county bureau is worried that the Construction Department will not agree, and intends to imitate the Zhenjiang method, collecting two months' rent from residents' shops, and will submit it to the county government meeting for discussion today (the 19th).

Changshu

A shop assistant committed suicide due to illness. Xu Chuanlong, a shop assistant at Houshengxiang Porcelain Shop, Xinpailou Dangko, South City, this county, is from Wujin County and is only twenty-eight years old this year. He suffered from a yin-yang typhoid fever due to his absurd behavior in the shop. He was lying in the shop, lacking people to take care of him, and his economy was not good. He was extremely worried and anxious, and suddenly had the idea of ​​being tired of the world. On the fourteenth of this month, Xu suddenly hired a rickshaw and ordered it to be pulled outside the West Gate. After the driver returned, he took advantage of the lack of attention and jumped into the river to commit suicide. The next morning, the shop suddenly received a report from the garrison outside the West Gate, saying that it had floated up in the Shanqiangtang. After going to recognize it, it was indeed Xu Chuanlong, so he reported to the county for verification and telegraphed his family to collect the body.

Xiaoyao You boat hall was sealed. There was a Xiaoyao You teahouse inside the West Gate of this county. The hall was located on the cliffs of the mountain, and the spring water was sweet. People in the county enjoyed going there to sip tea. Then manager Yuan Runsheng renovated the house into a playground style. Unexpectedly, since the renovation, it has suffered losses year after year. The various houses have been mortgaged separately to others. Now it is in a state of disuse. On the east side of the mountain, there is a boat hall, which is bright and airy and elegantly decorated. Two years ago, it was mortgaged to Bao Hai due to the loss of money. Bao was in charge, but the principal and interest were not repaid as scheduled. Bao had no choice but to go to seal and nail the boat hall the night before. From then on, anyone who sipped tea and Xiaoyao You was all closed.

Students from the Central Political School came to Changzhou for internship. Because the graduation period for students from the Central Political School in Nanjing is approaching, it was decided to send fourth-year students to various institutions across the country for internships. At the same time, the internship rules for each student were formulated, and the provincial and municipal governments were notified to follow them. Three people were assigned to the county government of this county: Li Yongbin from Suiyuan, Yuan Yongfu from Sichuan, and Fan Zubang from Shanxi. After arriving in Changzhou, it was decided to intern in various departments of the county government for a period of four months. During this period, they must not hold other positions or receive salaries. Various travel expenses, food, etc. are provided by the school. Once the internship period is over, they will be sent to various places for formal tasks.

Wuxi

The results of the examination in the rape case. Xie Axi, the sixteen-year-old daughter of Xie Dai, a woman in Workshop No. 1, Tatangxia, outside the South Gate of this county, was previously raped by Ye Ziping, an elderly man of sixty-one years old. The case was previously interrogated by Judge Liang of the County Court. As a result, the court ordered Xie Axi to be sent to Tongren Hospital for examination to determine whether she was a virgin. It is now known that Xie Axi was examined by Tongren Hospital yesterday and found that the hymen had been broken long ago. If she had intercourse with someone, it would not have been the first time. The hospital prepared an examination report and sent it back to the County Court. In the afternoon, Judge Liang summoned Xie Dai, the mother of Xie Axi, to the case, and signed and extracted Ye Ziping, who was in custody, to open the court for interrogation. He ordered Xie Dai to take Axi back to custody, and Ye Ziping was returned to custody to await a scheduled sentence.

Taifeng Silk Factory went on strike. Since its opening, Taifeng Silk Factory in Longchuanbang outside the West Gate of this county has been developing abnormally, but it is quite strict in terms of work, so the female workers are very dissatisfied. According to the usual practice, the weather has been hot recently, and various factories have changed to half-day work or triangular shifts, but only this factory is still working as usual. The female workers in the factory demanded that the factory change to half-day work the day before yesterday (the 17th), but the factory ignored them. Therefore, the female workers planned to deal with it and decided to go on strike unanimously. They could not resume work until they achieved their goal. It is currently being mediated.

A large number of floating corpses were found at Gaoqiaokou. A large number of floating corpses were suddenly found under the Gaoqiaokou River outside the North Gate of this county at 4 pm the day before yesterday (the 17th). There were a total of seven male and female corpses. The corpses were all tied with rough hemp ropes around their heads, shoulders, backs, etc., and there were wounds. The corpses had already rotted and were floating up and down. They were floated from the Taihu Lake area. After receiving the news, the Wuqiao Police Station of the Fifth Branch of Public Security, which is in charge, immediately ordered the police to investigate, but the floating corpses had already floated to other places and could not be found.

A fire broke out again in Huaishuxiang. Xu Yu, a resident of No. 4, Huaishuxiang, this city, her husband, Xu, has passed away long ago and has two sons, the eldest named Jin Da and the second named Mei Da, both of whom are masons and carpenters. They have two daughters, and their family is still doing well. Yesterday after lunch, the mother and son went to the field to cool off. How could the two little girls play with fire at home, which suddenly caused a fire? Before long, it broke through the roof. The nearby residents rang the gongs to warn, and the fire brigades from each district rushed to the scene and tried their best to extinguish the fire. It was only then that it was extinguished. Two rooms were burned down. When the fire was raging, Mei Da saw that the two little girls were still in the room, so he rushed into the room and rescued the two girls together. It was fortunate.

Changzhou

The bandit Wang Yaoting was captured. The bandit Wang Yaoting, who repeatedly committed kidnapping cases in various townships of Wuyi, has been wanted by the county government for a long time. The bandit fled to Shanghai and has not been captured. Police Captain Fang Qi recently learned that the bandit had recently sneaked back and was hiding in Xiguan Village, intending to cause trouble. He sent a team to join forces with Ge Qingda, the head of the Fucheng Township Security Regiment, and led the soldiers to capture him in three ways. After the team arrived in Xiguan Village, they saw the bandit escaping to the west of the village and crossing three rivers in a row. The team fired guns and chased him, and finally captured him in the river. He was sent to the security regiment for preliminary trial. On the 17th, he hired a boat to send him to the police team headquarters in the city. Then, because the bandit had confessed to the kidnapping cases he had committed and had two pistols and one rifle, he had recently sent one pistol to Jiang Lian, a member of the First Building outside the West Gate, for storage. Captain Fang immediately sent a team to search, but found nothing. He arrested Jiang Lian and questioned him. He confessed that the pistol had been thrown into the river at the Xidawang Temple. He also sent a team to search, but could not find it due to the deep and wide river. He sent Wang Yaoting and Jiang Lian, along with the confession, to the county and the Anti-Banditry Bureau for interrogation.

Yangzhou

The case of a civil servant enticing a singer in Yangzhou is a sensation. Shen Guinian and his wife, who lived at No. 27, Yongxing Street, Xincheng, were merchants and retired. They had a daughter named Yu Chun, who was twenty-nine years old and famous for her beauty. Because of poverty, Shen hired a teacher to teach his daughter songs and made her a singer in Yangfang Book House, Xinsheng Street, to make a living. Zhao Zhentan, an official of the Finance Bureau, listened to the songs and recognized the girl, and was surprised to find her pleasing. He used his monetary power to become a guest of the family. Zhao's brother-in-law, Bao, went back and forth with Zhao, and became familiar with her day by day. In June, he asked Shen and his wife for their daughter's hand on behalf of Zhao. Shen knew that Zhao already had a wife and refused outright, but Zhao was deeply in love with the girl and instigated her to leave. The girl was undecided. On the first of this month, Zhao went to Shen's house and invited the girl to go to Guanyin Mountain to offer incense, and then brought the girl to the Women's Relief Center. According to the rules, once one enters the center, one cannot leave. Shen Gu knew that Zhao had sisters who were female staff members in the center, and that Bao had resigned as the director of the center not long ago. He suddenly realized that this scene was planned by friends, so he filed a complaint with the county government, shouting for injustice. On the seventh, he received a reply: "It is known that Zhao Zhentan is a civil servant and dares to go out with prostitutes. It is not in line with officialdom. However, the matter of enticing wealth and beauty is within the scope of justice and should be prosecuted in the county court. The Finance Bureau should be ordered to dismiss Zhao Zhentan and send him to the court for interrogation and report. You should know this." After receiving this reply, Shen Gu shouted for injustice in various newspapers in Yangzhou, crying and begging for assistance from all walks of life, hoping to avoid the separation of mother and daughter. He went to Jiangdu County Court to file a criminal lawsuit. The prosecutor of the court has scheduled a hearing for 9 am on the 18th. Unexpectedly, another incident occurred. On the 14th, a "Shen Gu's Solemn Announcement" was published in the Jiangdu Daily under a false name. Shen was even more shocked, so he signed and sealed the announcement and published it in the Business Daily and other newspapers, and distributed flyers, pasted yellow lists, knocked on wooden fish, and shouted for injustice along the street, which led to the expansion of the case and caused a sensation in the society. All parties paid attention to it. Shen Gu also presented the case to the Governor's Office in Suijing because a certain sentence was serving as a consultant in the Office. Yesterday (the 16th), the Governor's Office suspended Bao and sent a team to Bao's residence to recover his badges.

Black stinky bugs were found on the crops. Black stinky bugs have suddenly appeared in the crops of Xinfeng District, Jiaxing, and are seriously harming the rice crops. The report has been reported to the provincial bureau for joint research on pest control methods so that it can be notified to each district and captured according to law.

Hangzhou

The Water Poisoning Case: Yesterday, the Xiaoshan East Gate Han Yuanchang copper and tin shop owner's wife, Lou Baozhen, who was accused of attempting to poison her husband, Han Yunsheng, by pouring poison into his teapot, was originally sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment by the county court. However, the prosecutor, dissatisfied with the verdict, appealed to the High Court. Lou Baozhen was escorted to Hangzhou, and after a court hearing and deliberation, the court overturned the original verdict and sentenced her to three years and three months of imprisonment.

Robbery at a Letter Agency: The Quansheng Letter Agency, located in front of the Tianhou Temple in Yongbu, has been in business for many years and its operations have been quite prosperous. On the fifteenth of this month, the agency instructed Chen Anguan and Ying Zhaoliang to hire a boat from Yong to transport letters, packages, and silver dollars worth 700 yuan to Yuyao. At around 7:00 PM, when the boat was passing the Nanhemu area near Xieqian Mountain, six or seven robbers suddenly appeared on another boat, each armed with a handgun. Letter Received

Letter from the Quanqiao Flood Relief Committee

To the esteemed editors of Shen Bao: Quanqiao has always been known as a barren land, and it has suffered successive years of famine. The scars of hardship have not yet healed, and there is no time for recuperation. At the beginning of the seventh month of this year, there were continuous torrential rains, causing mountain floods to erupt. The streets were flooded to a depth of six to seven feet, or four to five feet in some places. Most of the houses and walls of the common people collapsed, and grain was washed away. People and livestock drowned. The disaster victims had no place to live and no food to eat, and their cries for help were hoarse. All seventy-two weirs in the county were submerged, and the low-lying farmlands were also a vast expanse of water, leaving no hope for the autumn harvest. Subsequently, on the twenty-second day, there was a torrential downpour again, and after two days and nights of continuous rain, the floodwaters had not yet receded when a second devastating flood struck, even worse than the first. Areas near the city, such as Fuan Lane, Hewan, Xingtang Dam, Bai Wangtang, and Jinjia Orchard, were completely submerged. Houses collapsed, stoves were destroyed, and entire families were left without food. The waves were terrifying, and floating corpses were seen everywhere. The cries of mourning echoed in the fields. The lives of the people were left to the torrents of the flood, a scene of utter tragedy. Moreover, the farmlands in various districts were once again flooded, almost completely submerged. During the wind and rain, people were forced to sleep in the mud, and countless people contracted diseases and died. We implore you to publish this situation in the "Letters to the Editor" section and widely disseminate it, and to promote the fundraising and donation of benevolent porridge and righteous grains, for which we will forever be grateful for the kindness of rebirth. Respectfully submitted by the Quanqiao County Flood Relief Committee with seal.

Education News

Important News

Measures for Commemorating Children's Day

The Ministry of Education has formulated measures for commemorating Children's Day and issued a circular to the Education Departments and Bureaus of all provinces and cities, stating:

Regarding the proposal by the China Child Welfare Association to designate April 4th as Children's Day, the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan previously forwarded a letter to our Ministry for joint review with the Ministry of Interior. After joint discussion by the two ministries, it was deemed feasible and a response was sent for review and submission. Subsequently, Instruction No. 2174 of the Executive Yuan stated that the measures for commemorating Children's Day should be formulated and promulgated by the Ministry of Education. In addition to the Ministry formulating the measures for commemorating Children's Day and submitting them to the Executive Yuan for record and separate dispatch for implementation, a copy of the aforementioned measures is attached for the "Departments" and "Bureaus" to be informed and to instruct others to be informed of this order.

Measures for Commemorating Children's Day

(1) Purpose: The purpose of commemorating this day is to stimulate children's interest, inspire their love for the community, the country, and the family, and to raise social awareness of children's welfare. (2) Measures: A. All elementary schools (kindergartens) should carry out the following activities: 1. Give lectures on the anecdotes of revolutionary martyrs and ancient heroes of our country in their childhood (mainly to explain the virtues of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace) or the childhood lives of scientists and inventors in the world. 2. Perform games or short plays that inspire children's love for the community, the country, and the family (with special emphasis on parental love). 3. Print and distribute colored pictures about children's education and hygiene. 4. Give out Children's Day souvenirs to children (such as stationery, drawing supplies, etc., limited to students of the school or kindergarten). 5. Hold a parents' meeting for children in the school or kindergarten. 6. Hold a children's health competition or sports meet for the school or kindergarten. 7. Hold an exhibition of children's literary and artistic achievements in the school. In addition, various activities that can arouse interest, such as electing model children, may also be held. B. All social education institutions (such as public education centers) should carry out the following activities: 1. Convene a Children's Day commemorative conference (encouraging local people to bring their children to participate) and hold a Children's Day commemorative parade as appropriate. 2. Publicly exhibit various statistical charts on the local children's survey. 3. Hold an infant competition and a children's health or intelligence competition, and give prizes to the top winners as appropriate. 4. Give lectures on "The Responsibilities and Obligations of Parents," "Common Knowledge of (Protecting the Fetus), (Protecting Childbirth), (Protecting Infants)," "Methods of Training Wise Fathers and Good Mothers," and "The Necessity of Social Relief for Orphaned and Impoverished Children." 5. Join with local child welfare organizations (such as infant asylums and orphanages) and groups that seek the welfare of children to expand publicity on child welfare and child relief. 6. Print and distribute leaflets on "Children's Hygiene" and "Common Knowledge of (Protecting the Fetus), (Protecting Childbirth), (Protecting Infants)" and distribute them to parents. 7. Show films or plays about children's lives and welcome children to visit. 8. Art museums, museums, etc. in the local area should be specially opened to children and welcome them to visit. C. Advocate that each family should carry out the following activities at home on this day: 1. Hold a children's gathering for relatives and friends. 2. Hold a festival celebration where adults give gifts to children and older children give gifts to younger children (gifts should be limited to domestic products to arouse children's love for beauty, love for the community, and have scientific significance). 3. Prepare cakes and food specially steamed for Children's Day (the design of this kind of food should have educational significance) to add to the festive atmosphere. D. Advocate that children engage in the following appropriate games: (1) Flying kites (2) Playing stickball (3) Kicking shuttlecock (4) Other

The Songjiang County Education Association's Appeal for Songjiang Education Funds

▲Declaration The Songjiang County Education Association declares: Xu Xihuang, the Jiangsu Education County Administrative Investigation Commissioner, based on his subjective opinions and perverse actions, suddenly reduced the Songjiang education funds by more than 37,000 yuan and shut down more than 30 schools. Songjiang education has suddenly suffered a devastating blow, and it is difficult to defend against the blame. Upon investigation, the Songjiang education funds have always had savings and have never been in deficit. Instead of expanding, he is contracting. What is his intention? It is incomprehensible. The association feels deeply that the situation is critical and cannot remain silent. Therefore, meetings were held on July 14th and August 5th, and it was decided to separately submit appeals to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Ministry of Education, the Provincial Party Headquarters, the Provincial Government, the County Party Headquarters, the County Government, and the County Education Bureau, requesting assistance to maintain the original budget, inherit the legacy of invigorating education, strive for the spirit, and realize the claim so that the purpose can be achieved. This is the declaration.

▲Petition The petition from Tang Zhaoqiu, Chairman of the Songjiang County Education Assembly, to the National Government and other bodies states: "The petition is submitted because the education funds of Songjiang County have been arbitrarily reduced, making it difficult to maintain education. Please rectify the situation." (The petition is submitted jointly with the Songjiang County Government and the Education Bureau, requesting the Provincial Education Department to withdraw its order.) Upon investigation, although the education funds of Songjiang County are not abundant, they are sufficient to maintain education. After the 17th year, the funds for each school were allocated according to the minimum treatment standards of Sun Yat-sen University, and both parties were able to coexist peacefully. However, in the 19th year's budget, the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department suddenly reduced the funds, and the situation has already become difficult. However, due to strict orders, we have endured until now. In the 20th year's budget, after review, the staff of the schools are already complaining. Unexpectedly, the Education Department recently, based on the report of the Investigation Commissioner Xu Xihuang, further reduced the approved budget for the 20th year by a huge amount of 37,000 yuan, accounting for three-tenths of the county's education funds and shutting down more than 30 schools. The state of education is about to collapse. This association cannot sit idly by. Therefore, the first members' assembly was held on July 14th, and it was unanimously decided to separately submit appeals to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Ministry of Education, the Provincial Government, and the Provincial Party Headquarters, requesting rectification. Now, we present to the authorities the current state of education in Songjiang and the points where the investigation by Investigator Xu was negligent and did not conform to the facts. The funds for the senior division of elementary schools were calculated at 1,374 yuan per classroom per year according to the budget of the 17th year. In the 19th year's budget, the senior division was calculated at 1,119 yuan per classroom per year for Category A and 1,056 yuan for Category B, a reduction of 255 yuan to 318 yuan. In the approved budget for the 20th year, the senior division was calculated at 1,100 yuan per year for Category A and 978 yuan for Category B, a reduction of 84 yuan to 78 yuan compared to the 19th year and 339 yuan to 396 yuan compared to the 17th year. The junior division also experienced a similar decrease. Recently, according to the order of the Department, based on the report of Investigator Xu, and with reference to his proposed calculation, the senior division will be reduced by another 400 silver dollars per classroom, leaving only 700 yuan. In addition to the salaries of the teachers, there will be nothing left for other allowances and miscellaneous expenses. In the past, the schools in the towns and cities of the junior division were calculated at 24 students per classroom, deducting 48 yuan for tuition fees, and the schools in the rural areas deducted 24 yuan for tuition fees per class. Upon investigation, the amount of tuition fees collected by the junior division is extremely small, and sometimes even nothing is collected, and books and supplies must be given away. Now, Investigator Xu requires that the schools in the towns and cities calculate 35 students per classroom, deducting 70 yuan for tuition fees per year, and the rural areas calculate at 80% discount, with 28 students per classroom and deducting 56 yuan for tuition fees per year. In reality, this is difficult to achieve. In addition, the recurring expenses per class have been reduced by 40 yuan. Those who are clear-headed will be able to see whether this can be maintained. Upon investigation, our Songjiang secondary schools include the Provincial High School, the Provincial Girls' High School, the County High School, the County Normal School, and the Seven County Girls' Normal School. However, the Provincial High School and the Provincial Girls' High School also admit students from other provinces. The County Normal School will only recruit junior high school graduates in the future. The Girls' Normal School will not recruit students every year. Only the County High School can recruit as many students as possible. However, there are more than 400 elementary school graduates in this session, which is already more than the supply. However, Investigator Xu only knows to save funds and does not allow the County High School to open a double track in the first grade according to the established plan, only allowing it to recruit 50 new students, suddenly causing the students to be in danger of losing their education. The intention is difficult to understand. The students in the second grade of the County High School are more than 50 people, and a double class can be set up according to the regulations of the Ministry. Investigator Xu mistakenly counted only 49 people when he inspected, and should have merged them into one class in the 60th year, which is too much of an oversight. The County Training Instructors were originally set up as two people, so that it would be easier to train boys and girls separately, and the effect would be greater. However, Investigator Xu did not understand this and planned to reduce one person, which is not in line with the facts. Upon investigation, although the school buildings of the County Normal School are not spacious enough, adding one grade can be used as much as possible. Although the equipment is not complete, it is being gradually improved year by year. In order to implement teacher training, adapt to local needs, and provide a way out for students, it is appropriate to recruit elementary school graduates. However, Investigator Xu insisted on recruiting junior high school graduates, ignoring the need for normal education and local needs. This can be seen from this. The seven county girls' normal schools are limited to funds and education funds, only half of the other secondary schools, and only five corners of silver dollars per hour. Therefore, more teachers have to be hired to hold concurrent positions. However, the girls' normal schools, with limited funds, set up private classes in addition to public classes to remedy the shortage of teachers. The graduates of each session who serve in various schools have the best results. However, Investigator Xu only sees that there are fewer full-time teachers and criticizes them for resigning. Those with clear minds would never do this. In summary, the investigation by Investigator Xu either ignores the facts or is negligent and sloppy. It is difficult to get through, and it is self-evident. Upon investigation, the main point of Investigator Xu's huge reduction in education funds is that the budget for this year has a deficit of 101,000 yuan. In fact, the education funds of our Songjiang have always had savings and have never been in deficit. Even the newly levied mu tax is not moved without authorization. If it is as Investigator Xu said, why did the Education Bureau not submit a budget requesting a method to be discussed when it was not enough to make ends meet? Why did the Education Department approve it when reviewing the budget? Approval was given first, and reduction was given later. The orders were changed, and there was no way to know where to follow. Investigator Xu also said that the Songjiang collection agencies have a lot of arrears, such as one year's funds, which must be settled after two or three years, so that education funds cannot be received and spent appropriately. However, the funds for Year C, even if they are to be collected in Years D and E, can be collected in Year C for the funds for Years A and B. That is, the funds collected for arrears in Years A and B are used to make up for the arrears in Year C, and so on. There is originally no shortage, and it seems to be in deficit to clear it in one year. Investigator Xu also said that the reason for the deficit in Songjiang education funds is that the clerks are manipulating things, so the method of rectification should be designed from the tax collection aspect. But he does not think about the root and only orders the expenditures of each school to be reduced. If the clerks manipulate things one day and the education funds are completely cut off, will Investigator Xu order all the schools in Songjiang to close down completely? Perverse actions have reached this point. Investigator Xu also said that there is a lot of waste in the funds of each school, and it must be greatly reduced. However, the salaries of the teachers and staff in each school are all paid according to the prescribed amount, and there are receipts for other expenses. The recurring expenses are listed monthly and sent to the Economic Audit Committee for audit. The annual budget has also been approved and reduced. I don't know what the saying of waste refers to. In short, Investigator Xu indulged in his subjective opinions, ignoring the facts, the plan was wrong, and education was destroyed. It is a clear violation of the late Premier Sun's legacy of revitalizing education, a disregard for the National Assembly's proposal to raise salaries, and the fault of dereliction of duty is difficult to defend. This association is in a leading position and cannot bear to see Songjiang education fall into a desperate situation. It has no choice but to present the truth and request the Ministry (Government) to instruct the Education Department to rectify it immediately, so as to create talents and lay the foundation for the country. All the reasons why the education funds of Songjiang have been arbitrarily reduced and are difficult to maintain and Investigator Xu has insisted on his own way and ignored the facts are reported separately. This document is prepared to be submitted to your departments for review and compliance. Respectfully submitted to the National Government, the Central Party Headquarters, the Provincial Government, the Provincial Party Headquarters, the Ministry of Education, the County Government, the County Education Bureau, the County Party Headquarters, the Chairman of the Songjiang County Education Association Members' Assembly, Tang Shaoqiu.

News on the Preparations for the Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society

The eighth annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society will be held in Ningbo from September 1st to September 7th. It is reported that the preparations for this event have been entrusted by the society to local officials and gentry in Ningbo to handle, and they have been very thorough. It has been learned that the itinerary arranged by the preparatory committee includes tours of famous scenic spots such as Fenghua Xuebao, Tiantong Temple, Yiwang Temple, and Putuo Mountain. The committee has also instructed famous scenic spots and temples to provide accommodation and meals, so that members will not have to make arrangements individually, which would waste time and money. Therefore, the annual meeting fee charged to members this year is five yuan higher than in previous years. The sedan chairs used to visit the four famous scenic spots will also be arranged by the preparatory committee. Members who wish to attend the meeting must notify County Magistrate Chen of Yin County a few days in advance, so that he can arrange the sedan chair fee, which will cost about twelve yuan per person. Accommodation and meals in Ningbo will be arranged by the members themselves. It is reported that the budget prepared by the preparatory committee has been submitted to Ma Yinchu, the president of the society, who is very satisfied. According to Mr. Ma, the total amount of the budget is no more than 3,000 yuan, including sedan chair fees, boat fees, and accommodation and meals for the four famous scenic spots. However, accommodation and meals in Ningbo are arranged by individuals and are not included in the budget. If the society were to handle it itself, it would cost more than 4,000 yuan. It has now been resolved by the board of directors that members attending the meeting will share about 2,000 yuan, and the general office will allocate more than 1,000 yuan. Calculating with 100 people, each person will only pay about 21-22 yuan. All the accommodation, meals, sedan chair fees, boat fees, tips, and public banquets for the four places are included. Compared with individuals traveling on their own, the cost is only one-third, it is said.

The National Mandarin Education Discussion Conference Closed Yesterday

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association convened the National Mandarin Discussion Conference and the 20th Annual General Meeting. The second discussion meeting was held yesterday at Moore Hall, and the closing ceremony of the General Meeting was held. The following is a record of the news:

(1) Second General Meeting

The second discussion meeting started at 8:30 AM yesterday. Wu Jingheng (represented by Lu Yiyan) presided over the meeting and performed the formalities. (1) Reported the number of attendees. (2) The chairman of the review committee reported the review results. (3) Began the discussion.

The following motions were passed: 1. The sixteenth motion of the first category was passed according to the review results. 2. The thirty-eighth and thirty-ninth motions of the second category were passed according to the review results. 3. The forty-fourth, forty-first, forty-sixth, forty-third, and forty-fourth motions of the third category were passed according to the review results. 4. The eighteenth, nineteenth, and thirty-third motions of the fourth category were passed according to the review results. 5. The fifty-seventh, fifty-eighth, fifty-ninth, and sixtieth motions of the fifth category were passed according to the review results.

▲Temporary Motions (1) The sixty-first motion, "Select new teaching materials and submit them to the Ministry of Education for circulation to all provincial departments for distribution to schools in counties, cities, villages, and districts for separate adoption." (Wang Huizhou, Ying Jie) It was resolved that this case be sent to the Propaganda Department of the National Mandarin Education Promotion Association to introduce new Mandarin teaching materials as much as possible. (2) The sixty-second motion, "Petition the Ministry of Communications to order all post offices in the country to quickly correct the Mandarin Romanization stamps and add phonetic symbols to remove obstacles to the promotion of Mandarin." (Ni Qianyuan) It was resolved that it be passed. (3) The sixty-third motion, "Petition the Ministry of Education to order all provincial, city, and county educational administrative agencies to hold large-scale Mandarin sports meetings at least twice a year to promote popularization." (Ni Qianyuan) It was resolved that it be sent to the Propaganda Department of the National Mandarin Education Promotion Association for reference. (4) The sixty-fourth motion, "Petition the Ministry of Education to order all schools at all levels to add phonetic symbols or Mandarin Romanization to the entrance examinations." (Peng Jianong) It was resolved that the main text be changed to "Petition the Ministry of Education to order all schools at all levels to add phonetic symbols or Mandarin Romanization to the entrance examinations or graduation examinations." (5) The sixty-fifth motion, "Petition the Ministry of Education to order all bookstores in the country to publish scripts with Mandarin pronunciations and add tonal symbols." (Xiao Chongwu) It was resolved that it be merged with the forty-ninth motion. (6) The sixty-sixth motion, "Please promote the National Central Research Institute to revise the phonetic alphabet." (Zhou Yingjie) It was withdrawn by the original proposer. (7) It was resolved to organize a motion review committee.

▲Elected Committee After the discussion was over, Wang Shaoyu, representative of the Education Department of Hebei Province, Chen Jianheng, representative of the Education Department of Shandong Province, Wang Dexi, representative of the Education Department of Anhui Province, Li Zhengkai, representative of the Education Department of Jiangxi Province, Han Shoujin, representative of the Education Department of Jiangsu Province, Zhang Kejun, representative of the Education Department of Zhejiang Province, Wang Zuyou, representative of the Education Department of Hubei Province, Wang Yongrong, representative of the Education Department of Fujian Province, Xu Gongmei, representative of the Education Bureau of Nanjing, and Chen Yu, representative of the Education Bureau of Shanghai, were elected as members. (2) Li Zhengkai, representative of the Education Department of Jiangxi Province, Wang Luji, representative of the Education Department of Hebei Province, and Yi Xiwu delivered speeches in succession. Yesterday's Results

China, Canada, Japan, and Portugal quarterfinals starting Saturday

The Rotary Cup International Tennis Tournament has ended its fierce preliminary round. Canada eliminated the United States 3-0, and Japan also eliminated the powerful England 3-2. Japan took an early lead of 2-1. In the last two singles matches yesterday morning, the result was one win and one loss. Therefore, the total score was 3-2.
