Free Talk

Small Things in the World

— Hai Ke

The World's Slowest Breathing Person

All human beings breathe between fifteen and eighteen times per minute. This is generally the case. However, in Baltimore, USA, there is a woman who only breathes three to five times per minute.

Her slow breathing was not noticed at first. Five or six years ago, when she was studying physiology at university, she discovered that her breathing was not as fast as that of her classmates. The degree of slowness broke all previous records. A famous doctor, who had visited twenty cities in Europe and lectured on medicine to 70,000 medical professionals, said that he had never encountered a person who breathed so slowly.

The average person inhales only one pint of air per breath, while this woman can inhale three pints each time. Her lungs are no different from those of an average person, and not larger than others. If she were to go swimming, she could stay underwater for a particularly long time. And when she sings, her voice can be extended for a particularly long time.

Jasmine Jottings

— Chen Yiwei

Of the flowers of the four seasons, many are lovely. In this scorching summer, the lotus and water lily excel in their beautiful names, appreciated by poets and hermits, and often found in poems and writings. Among them, the jasmine flower is no less beautiful than other flowers, and its wide use surpasses them all, often seen in new words and phrases.

Jasmine comes from the Western Regions. Its translated name is Yesiming, and it is also named Suxin for its similar species. Later, the pointed-petal species was called Yesiming, and the round-petal species was called Jasmine. The leaves are as large as cups, and the flowers are as small as beans. The color is pure white, and the fragrance is very strong. It is mostly grown in Fujian and Guangdong. Today, the species grown in Fujian are mostly round-petal. In the past, Lu Jia's "Records of a Journey to the South" said that the five grains of Nanyue were tasteless and the hundred flowers were not fragrant, only the jasmine did not change with the water and soil. From this, the value of this flower in the South can be seen.

The method of planting is that spring is the right time, and the soil should be loose, mixed with sand is even better. When the stems are long and the leaves are lush, only water is needed, and no nutrients are required. It can naturally bud and bloom, and its labor is quite economical. Whether planted in pots or in gardens, it can grow. Its benefits are even easier to reap.

It has special advantages among all flowers. All flowers must be inserted in a vase after being picked and nourished with water to bloom and not wither. The jasmine is different. Pick its buds, without connecting the stems, string them with thread, like a string of beads. The flowers bloom and do not wither for several days, or tie them to the handle of a fan. The fan moves and the fragrance is born, refreshing the heart and lungs. Or hang it on a chimney, the fragrance follows the smoke, lingering and fragrant. Or tie it into tassels, knotted in the embroidered couch, so that the land of black sleep becomes a fragrant city. It can also be used as a woman's ornament. Those who have not cut their hair wear it as a hairpin. Those who have cut their hair wear it as a forehead ring, so that the beautiful jade face and the bright flower face reflect each other and are both beautiful. The "Book of Jin" says that the people of the capital wear the Nai flower as a mourning band for the Weaver Girl. In the north, jasmine is called Nai. Thus, the use of jasmine as decoration by women in the north has been around for a long time.

The most extensive source of profit is tea making. Fine and expensive teas, such as Sparrow Tongue and other varieties, are generally scented with jasmine, so that the tea tastes fragrant and delicious. Pick out the remaining ones and bake them into scented tea, so the taste of scented tea is inferior to it. The Nine Miles in Guangzhou is called Flower Field. The Fenggang area in the southern district of Fuzhou is also called Flower Field. Flower pickers take advantage of the faint morning light, when the buds contain dew, and carry baskets and baskets to pick them. Until the setting sun hangs down, the carriers and pickers flock to the market, throwing them into the tea houses for sale. Some villagers specialize in this profit and can earn more than a thousand yuan a year.

People in Fujian often write jasmine as Jili, which is wrong. Mu is alfalfa, which is used to feed cattle and horses. It is not the same species as jasmine. I will attach it at the end to correct the error.

Visit to Hongzheng Altar

— Langgan

Humans and ghosts have different interests. The living and the dead have different paths. Confucian scholars do not talk about gods and monsters. Confucius said that he did not know life, how could he know death? The sages still made such remarks, let alone ordinary people. However, there are indeed unbelievable things in the world. Physical laws and common sense are not always sufficient. However, the facts are clear and the miracles are obvious, which are what people do not want to believe but have to believe. Automatic writing is one of them. My friend Xie Junwenrong has always been a theist and is a firm believer in this path. He is a disciple of Hongzheng Altar and often tells me about the spiritual efficacy of automatic writing, firmly inviting me to watch and prove that his words are not false. So last week, I accompanied Sun Jun to visit the altar. The altar is located in Qingxiang Lane, Jielu, a very narrow place. Climbing the stairs, turning several times, we reached the room. The incense smoke was swirling, and the people wanted to choke. The walls were hung with portraits of gods and automatic writing. The portraits of Ji Gong and Chunyang had clear features and were clearly recognizable, said to have been taken from space. This is one strange thing. We sat for about half an hour, and then the automatic writing began. The people in the room all held their breath and waited, very devout. At first, countless circles were drawn in the sand tray, not forming words. Then the hands of the one holding the planchette moved greatly, and gradually they could be recognized. Today happened to be the birthday of the Goddess of Mercy. All the gods and immortals went to celebrate. The altar master Ji Gong was not back from the South China Sea. The words "Keeping the Altar with an Inch of Incense" appeared in the sand tray, instructing us to wait a little longer and then try again. So everyone retreated to rest. First, my companions and I made an agreement with Xie Jun that we should ask the god about our fortune and misfortune, so as to divine our fate. Jun then asked the person in charge to take a yellow slip and write down our names and the matters we wanted to ask about. My two companions and I each wrote one, asking about our lifelong fortune and misfortune, and asking the god to give us a poem. Both yellow slips were placed on the altar table. After an inch of incense had passed, we reopened the table. At this time, the altar master Ji Gong also returned. After writing about twenty or thirty words, he addressed the matters we had asked about. Staring at the sand tray, the strokes danced like dragons and snakes, and could not be read to the end. The one holding the planchette would make a word with his hand, then call it out and order the recorder to write it down. After it was finished, we looked at it. The first and second lines were all six characters, and the third line was seven characters. Moreover, it was a poem given to both of us. The original text said: "Miao miao zhun er guo, wu yu tui chu chuang men. Yi shi xia yu su lin tou, qie dai he shi zi zu". What exactly is the meaning of this? After thinking hard, I could not understand it. I was very confused. A few days ago, I met Mr. Ding Zhonghu, a recluse in the fields, and asked him about automatic writing. The gentleman said bluntly, "I dare not say that Ji Gong and Chunyang exist. I dare not say that the theory of the soul is necessarily absent." He then told me about the story of Mr. Hu Junyanfu in "Common Talk Series." Hu Junyanfu taught in a private school at home. One day, a guest arrived. He was about to send someone to buy food for the guest. He made a list of items on paper, but when he started writing, he felt that the strokes were horizontal and vertical, and he could not write as he wanted. He was very frightened, thinking that he was sick. But when he put down the pen, his hand was normal, and there was no pain. When he picked up the pen again, it was as before. The guest said, "This is probably automatic writing." I have seen the state of those who practice automatic writing, and it is exactly like this. Gu Jun has never practiced automatic writing and does not believe it. At that time, several Confucian scholars of the clan gathered together and taught him to hold the pen loosely and write at will. Then the characters were as big as bowls, skewed, clumsy, and rough. When they looked at them, they recognized the three characters "Zeng Zigu". Everyone was surprised and said that Mr. Nanfeng had come. So they burned incense and paid their respects, asking him to write a poem. He refused, saying that he was unable to. They sighed in regret. People said that Nanfeng was good at prose but short on poetry, which was not false. Then they asked him about the works recorded in the collection. He also refused, saying that he had forgotten them all for a long time. Everyone was already suspicious. That day happened to be the spring festival, so they took it as the subject and forced him to write a poem. He wrote a five-character quatrain, which was very vulgar. They asked if he could make art, and he said he could. They pointed to the topic of the day and asked him to try, but he could not write smoothly. Everyone laughed and stopped. The next day, holding the pen was as before, but the characters were slightly more correct. He wrote a brief narrative as he had done at first. They asked if he was still Zigu, and he said no. The one who came yesterday was an impersonator. He was a certain villager who had given up his career early. As for me, I was a student of the Imperial College in the world. I had learned the Eight-Part Essay and completed an article. He also told them his residence and name in great detail. Everyone knew that it was a ghost. Compared to the one who came yesterday, his writing was slightly more understandable. When asked about things, his answers were also in line with people's expectations, and there was nothing strange. He came as soon as he picked up the pen, and his words were trivial. I was tired and thanked him. However, he still came from time to time. One night, lying in bed, his hands were shaking. Jun was deeply worried about being disturbed, and the family members were even more frightened when they heard about it. They quickly moved the bed home and moved the museum. Since then, it has stopped. There was nothing else after that.

The World's Richest Man

— Yan Ye

The Indian Nizam has assets of 1 billion US dollars, making him the richest man in the world. His 1 billion dollars are mostly in jewelry and gold. This huge fortune is not stored in a secure bank vault but is hidden at home. He resides in Hyderabad, a remote and wild area. To ensure the safety of his treasures, he built a city wall around his house, with well-trained and strong men guarding it, and heavy cannons and sharp guns. The place is as solid as a golden pond, and thieves and robbers cannot even get a glimpse of it. The Nizam is extremely stingy and does not donate to any charitable causes. However, he often gives servants thousands or even tens of thousands of dollars during the holidays. People find this strange. He also told people, "I can dispose of my property according to my free will. If my son is like me, I will give it to him. If he is not what I love, then I will give it to the world. It can be scattered in an instant. Now I still have the ability to protect it. Heaven has given me a huge fortune, and I must fulfill my responsibility to protect it. If I have the ability to protect it but entrust it to others, I am failing Heaven. If I do not have the ability to protect it but do not entrust it to those who can bear this responsibility, I am also failing Heaven. Therefore, my responsibility to protect it cannot be removed now. Even if it is removed, I have not found someone to entrust it to." Today's commentators on respecting property say that property should be used as much as possible for the purpose of creating wealth and benefiting society, the country, and the people. The Nizam's words and deeds are contrary to this. It is also said that the wealth of the world is mainly in the United States, and the most millionaires are also in the United States. However, even the four richest people in the United States, such as Ford, each have only 500 to 600 million dollars, so they are not comparable to the Nizam. This is why the Nizam is the richest man in the world.

Travels in India (84)

— Linghua

The national movement of the Indian people began in 1889. However, it was only able to make reports to the government. It was not until after the Russo-Japanese War from 1909 to 1911 that the Indians realized that the small Asians could defeat the large European powers, let alone the large India. After the Chinese Revolution, the Indians were determined to start an uprising. The Gandhi movement has been going on for more than 20 years, and its effectiveness has been in recent months. The progress in recent months has been greater than in the previous 20 years. The senior officials are all British. The middle-level officials with power are also British, interspersed with idle positions belonging to the Indians. The real power of the lower-level officials still belongs to the British. Only the police belong to the Indians. The British spend 600 million rupees a year on raising troops. However, the British troops are not visible in peacetime, to show their civilization and generosity. Once something happens, they arrive like a storm, to show their unpredictability. They are mostly stationed in the north to defend against China and Russia. The Indians are like sheep and have no defense to speak of.

Indian geography is roughly divided into three parts. One is the Himalayan Mountains, which is a cold region in the far north. Its inhabitants are very dense, close to Chinese Tibet. Indians also call Tibet China. The second is the Ganges River Basin, from Calcutta to Lahore. The Ganges River Basin is a land of political, religious, rich, and strong people, and is also the center of people. The third is the desert south of the Ganges River, the southern Indian provinces.

The old people, students, children, ladies, and monks I met all liked to hear about Chinese affairs and liked to come to China. I don't know why. I feel that everything has a natural opportunity. When the opportunity arrives, it is beyond human control. The feeling of India towards China has several reasons. One is due to external pressure, so they think of sympathizing with those who show sympathy for them. They know that the Buddha left India and went to China, and China is their first sympathetic friend. It is a large country with a large population and no ambitions. They feel that Japan, China, and Siam are all Buddhist countries, and Japan is strong, so they sigh and miss China and love the Chinese. Because the Chinese spread Indian culture to the world, and also act as the host of India. These feelings arise spontaneously. The British suppress us, and the Chinese bathe in the grace of the Heavenly Abode and are liberated in body and mind, eliminating our many disasters. The country has been peaceful and the people have been safe for thousands of years. Now they know that they should repay their kindness, which is their duty. If the Indians can come, they should be greeted with flowers and music. The Buddhist societies and monasteries in various places are all their combined halls. In the past, Tagore asked me for the fruits of the old trees for thousands of years. Now is the time. China is the crown of Asian culture. Support India, revive the Jews, unite the Muslims, revive Siam, and destroy all differences to win the hearts of the world. Is this not the duty of the Chinese nation in the 20th century?

Rotary Club Speech

Women, Women (24)

— Yao Sufeng

Little Rong's wife was in the back room, and had long heard her husband come in. The fire in her heart could no longer be suppressed. She was about to jump out and question him, but Qiu Zi persuaded her. She also remembered what Miss Ding had told her earlier, and had to endure the anger in her stomach, and remained there.

However, from the crack in the door, she saw her husband's gentle attitude towards Miss Ding, and couldn't help but think of his violent behavior the last time he came home to get money. Her eyes could no longer see anything clearly, and her heart became even more depressed and resentful.

But at this time, in Miss Ding's mind, Mr. Lu was like a naive magician performing in front of a smart audience. The magic that had been exposed no longer had any appreciation. However, this magician himself did not know it, and he even thought there were people still watching his new tricks.

He suddenly stood up, walked to Miss Ding, and said even more softly, "I have some things today that I want to discuss with you, but I can't seem to say them."

"What is it?" Miss Ding replied coldly.

"A relative came to Shanghai, because my father asked him to buy some things, but he didn't bring enough money. He came to discuss it with me. It just so happens that I'm running out of money too, and the family hasn't sent it yet, so I have to turn to you for help. Please lend me a hundred silver dollars temporarily. When the money from my family arrives the day after tomorrow, I will return it to you immediately," Mr. Lu said with a smile in every sentence.

"Very convenient—but let me ask someone to get it for you! Because it's inconvenient for me right now." Miss Ding also forced an unnatural smile, because she clearly knew that this was still a set of ridiculous magic tricks.

So she stood up and pulled Mr. Lu towards the back room. The door opened, and Mr. Lu was suddenly struck by the sight of his wife in front of him, as if he had been hit by a heavy mallet.

When Little Rong's wife saw Little Rong come in, she couldn't bear it anymore and immediately jumped forward and grabbed him.

Miss Ding, however, said with a sneer, "Mr. Lu, the hundred silver dollars you want, please discuss it with that lady! What do you think?"

Mr. Lu could no longer tolerate it. He was ashamed and angry, and pushed his right hand hard, and his wife fell to the ground. He said loudly, "How did you get here?"

Little Rong's wife lay on the ground and cried loudly. She also said with great anger, "I was just about to ask you! How did you get here?"

▲ Market Conditions Are Uncertain Yesterday, the 18th, the Specie Fluctuated Unpredictably. Foreign Rice Price Report Declines

▲ 6.5 to 6.9 Mace

After the price of various domestic rice types in this city rose some days ago, various domestic merchant groups competed to purchase foreign rice. Japanese merchants also speculatively placed orders, and the price at the origin immediately showed repeated increases. In addition, due to high gold prices, it was difficult to place orders profitably. Yesterday, foreign merchants and Chinese merchants received a telegram from Annam, reporting that the market price at the origin had slightly decreased, with quotations for No. 1 Saigon rice ranging from 6.5, 6.67 mace, to 6.89 mace. A bid price of 6.5 mace has already been telegraphed out, and it is expected to be transferred approximately tomorrow or the day after.

Flour Market Returns to Weakness

▲ Although there are floods, transportation is not open ▲ Inland Yangtze merchant groups are mostly withdrawing

Yesterday, the flour market, after opening in the morning and afternoon, the prices for each month tended towards a quiet trend again. The quotation for foreign wheat once decreased by about 0.2 taels. As for the inland Yangtze merchant groups, they have been gradually purchasing smoothly for over a month, and the quantity is truly enormous. Now, although disasters are continuous, it is like a vast ocean, and land and water transportation have not yet recovered. Even if they purchase spot goods, they cannot promote sales. Therefore, the mindset of these groups has turned to slackness, and quite a few are withdrawing. Observing the future, perhaps sales are difficult to stimulate due to actual difficulties, and the weakness must continue. As a result, this month fell by 0.075 taels compared to the previous day, September fell by 0.0125 taels, October and November fell by 0.01, December fell by 0.0125 taels, and January fell by 0.005 taels.

Wheat Market Near Weak, Far Flat

Yesterday, the futures wheat market, after opening in the morning and afternoon, each month showed a trend of near weak and far flat. This month, due to outsiders withdrawing, the market trend was sluggish. Because the short sellers' attitude was very firm, most were prepared to deliver. September also showed a flat and weak trend due to the Han merchant group withdrawing. From October to December, buying and selling were balanced, with no fluctuations. January also saw a decline due to very quiet buying interest. As a result, August, September, and January each fell by over 0.03 taels and remained unchanged. The current wheat market situation is that arrivals are still not very smooth, factory purchases are slightly better, and prices are similar to the previous day. Over 2,000 packages of wheat from the opening of Taicang, Kunshan, Anting, Chongming, Waigang, Wusong, and Pudong were handled by Fuxin Huafeng.

Sugar Market Unified Disc, Gradually Rising

▲ Cotton Lake Red Opens Quite Well

Yesterday's sugar market production area telegrams showed that Cuban current sugar prices have not changed. New York futures sugar for September and December each rose by 0.02 taels compared to the previous telegram. March and May of next year each fell by 0.02 taels. Java current futures sugar still lacks ups and downs. In the Association market, the buying interest for Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse sand white was slightly active, with old goods priced at 11.45 to 11.5 taels, and new white goods priced from 11.6 taels, rising to as high as 11.7 taels, and the market shape was still firm. No. 20 medium sand white was quoted at 11.1 taels, with very few takers. Bowl blue was at 8.75 taels, and several hundred bags were traded, with a clear trend. Taikoo sugar also saw a gradual rise, with B mark at 12.15 taels, HM mark at 11.5 to 11.025 taels, back market at 11.55 taels, CW mark old goods at 12 taels, PX mark at 10.04 taels, O mark at 9.4 taels, and the market situation was still stable. Hua Xin offered to sell 1,000 bags of current old coarse sand white at a price of 11.45 taels. The market inventory of domestic Cotton Lake red sugar is very scarce. Several dozen packages were opened yesterday, and the price rose to 11.7 taels, and the market was stable and refined.

Northern and Southern Goods, Lanxi Honey Dates Arrive in Volume, Prices Fall

Lanxi honey dates, since the new crop came out, initially sold for 40 taels due to the small quantity. Now that the source has reached a scale of 400 pieces, the price has gradually decreased. Yesterday, the market was only selling for 32 taels. However, this year's output is particularly abundant, and this price is not yet a low level, so the future market is still difficult to be optimistic about, and there is a possibility of continued decline.

Silk and Tea, Jinhua Autumn Silkworm Hatching and Seeding Smooth

Farmers in various cities and villages under the old Jinhua Prefecture have suffered greatly from the damage caused by the weather to the spring and summer silkworms this year. The silkworm business has suffered huge losses, and most are preparing to raise autumn silkworms, ordering improved seeds from the provincial silkworm farms to engage in hatching. Recently, the weather has been sunny and the wind is gentle and the sun is warm, which is very suitable for the progress of silkworm farming. Large groups have already collected ants and urged them to turn green, which is quite smooth.

Needle Eyebrow Pearl Tea, Sales to Europe Smooth

Yesterday, the European dealers' interest in green tea such as needle eyebrow, show eyebrow, hemp pearl, and shrimp eye from Wuyuan and Tunxi was intense. The entire market transaction was quite lively, and the selling price was also better by 2 or 3 taels. The top price of Phoenix eyebrow has already opened to 95 taels, which is a high price not seen recently. As for the precious eyebrow market, it is slightly quiet, probably because British and French firms, in view of the recent sharp rise, have had to slow down their progress to try to suppress it, but the Chinese merchants have always been firm, and the market price has not risen or fallen compared to last week.

Piece Goods, Recent Woolen Cloth News

The trade in woolen goods and woolen cloth has been in a quiet period recently. Yesterday, the buyers had pre-purchase news for the thick woolen goods sold in autumn and winter. Quite a few camel wool transactions were made, with Weilon, Xianda, Shengda, Hongfa, Tianxiang, and Wei Yi domestic goods strips selling for 2.15 taels, plain colors for 1.65 taels, delivered in Shanghai, with an additional silver dollar of 0.01 taels per yard for export. Other printed rotten wool, overcoat wool, leopard skin, black velvet, sable otter velvet, etc., were also inquired about. Most of the successful negotiations were limited to delivering silver and goods next month. White drill, white straight tribute, baleni, miyale, yellow twill, fine twill adhesive cloth, feather yarn and the like all lack buyers. Yuan Changqing gray, dark green plain drill, coming color Huate cloth, checkered Huate cloth, oblique dot chocolate, Yuan Qing straight tribute cloth, etc., all had transactions. Drill with 2.2 to 2.3 taels grades was popular, Yuan straight tribute with 5 taels customs clearance was popular, and the lower the grade of Huate cloth chocolate the more popular.

Hardware, New Iron Goods Arrive in Volume, Sales Stagnant

Among the new iron goods, such as tinplate, British steel plate, French nails, angle iron, flat white iron, cigarette iron, new foreign yuan, bamboo steel, etc., in the past three or four days, more than 26,000 dan have been shipped one after another, and the inventory was temporarily full, so the customers who wanted to purchase were hesitant to move forward, so the entire market trading was quite quiet.

Automobile News

Special Article

The Widespread Automobile Manufacturing Industry

— Pei

The automobile is undoubtedly the finest craft in modern manufacturing. This is common knowledge. The materials used are available everywhere in the world, almost as if they are lying around for the taking. However, fewer people know this fact. Some even believe that the American automobile industry is the most developed, with the largest sales volume, and that American-made cars are sold in every country in the world. Therefore, they assume that America is the main base for automobile manufacturing because all the materials for automobile production are produced in the United States. This is not true.

In fact, the automobile manufacturing industry is an international product. The materials used in its production are produced everywhere. Therefore, people all over the world, whether directly or indirectly, depend on supplying materials for automobile manufacturing. In some areas, there are countless thousands of people involved. Thus, the forests, mines, farms, and factories in Africa, Asia, Europe, America, Oceania, and the Far East contribute significantly to the creation of a single automobile. To achieve excellence in automobile production, it is essential to seek various quality materials extensively. Other important minerals used in automobile manufacturing include: steel from North America; aluminum from Canada or South America; copper from Chile, Africa, and the Americas; tin from Malaysia and Bolivia; and nickel from Canada. However, the materials needed for automobile manufacturing are not limited to these. Wood, rubber, and silk are all necessary. Wood, used for building the car body and various accessories, comes mostly from forests around the world. Hardwood, in particular, is shipped from Central America. Rubber, used for making tires and electrical wires, comes from various Eastern countries. Wool is also used in large quantities in automobile manufacturing, often in thousands of pounds annually. Australia, Argentina, and Uruguay are the suppliers of this product. Silk is mostly shipped from Japan. Leather comes from livestock-raising areas, such as Australia and Argentina. Asbestos is supplied by Canada. High-quality cotton, known for its strength and resilience, is often used in the production of the best tires. This high-quality cotton comes from Egypt. Cork comes from Spain.

Various alloys and metals are used extensively in automobile manufacturing, often being specialties of specific regions. Manganese comes from Brazil, Russia, and India. Barium, a necessary component for batteries, comes from China and Mexico. Button steel comes from Peru. Tungsten comes from China. Molybdenum is mostly found in North America. Mercury is used extensively in automobile manufacturing and comes from Spain, Italy, Turkey, and Mexico. Steel used for manufacturing small, exquisite parts and testing tools is of high quality and comes from Switzerland. Recently, in the automobile manufacturing industry, there has been a high demand for materials used in manufacturing alloys and metal plates. However, this important metal is only produced in Rhodesia in central South Africa. Next are paint and gum, which mostly come from the Far East. New Zealand and tropical regions also produce them. Linseed oil, used for making oil, comes from Argentina and is essential for paint. Coarse paint, used as a base material, comes mostly from Italy and Spain, including shades and light colors. All of the above are directly related to automobile manufacturing. In addition, there are countless indirect supplies. Gasoline and other fuels are produced in various countries. The automobiles we see today are made with the highest quality materials. Their creation involves meticulous planning and is a crystallization of sophisticated craftsmanship. The manufacturing process follows a specific sequence: casting metal, creating molds, manufacturing parts, making machinery, and then proceeding to the car body. The final step is to assemble the various components to complete the automobile. Each step is executed with precision. Therefore, the manufacturing process incorporates scientific equipment and techniques that are unmatched by other manufacturing industries. Moreover, the pursuit of product excellence and cost-effective production are additional considerations. The results seen today demonstrate a high degree of perfection. However, the art of manufacturing is constantly refined, and innovation and improvement continue to advance daily without end. Once an automobile is manufactured and enters the market for public use, there is a sense of romance involved. Describing it in detail would be very interesting, but it would require too much paper and ink. Let's consider just one aspect. Everyone knows that automobiles are used for transportation. However, after an automobile is manufactured and leaves the factory to reach the market, it must also rely on transportation. Therefore, trains and ships are indispensable intermediaries. Similarly, the supply of automobile manufacturing materials relies on various transportation methods. Thus, whether directly or indirectly, mining, forestry, farming, manufacturing, and sales are all related to automobiles, providing employment for millions of people. Other related industries include road construction and bridge building. Generally speaking, the production of various regions and the work of various peoples are related to the automobile manufacturing industry in some way. As for the use of automobiles, broadly speaking, they are related to the national economy and the people's livelihood. Narrowly speaking, they are essential necessities in people's daily lives. Simply put, they can be called "manufacturers of happiness." Therefore, since the invention of the automobile, human evolution has been greatly influenced. The automobile is not to be overlooked.

Astonishing Achievements of the Vauxhall Car

Not only beautiful in appearance, but also in line with economic principles

The automobile industry today has reached a peak. However, in Europe and America, the number of automobile factories has become as numerous as carp crossing a river. Therefore, competition among the factories for business is fierce. If a factory falls behind in the competition, its business prospects are at risk of failure. This is why each factory must strive for excellence in the manufacturing of its vehicles, in order to achieve a significant position in the market. Recently, when factories manufacture cars, they not only demand beauty in appearance, but their main goal is to make vehicles that align with economic principles. Otherwise, they cannot effectively compete. Currently, there are many products from various factories that meet these principles, but the Vauxhall is particularly outstanding among them. The Vauxhall has long enjoyed a considerable reputation in the automobile industry. In 1930 alone, the Vauxhall was ranked as the number one new car produced by British factories. The reason for this is that, after the Vauxhall was introduced to the world, it underwent several long and short distance test drives, as well as automobile races. The results proved that it was not only aesthetically pleasing, but also the most economical vehicle on the market. This was truly unexpected.

The Vauxhall's ability to align with economic principles lies in its affordable price and excellent materials. Furthermore, after purchasing a new car, the owner can immediately see that the Vauxhall saves on all sorts of consumption compared to ordinary cars. Therefore, after the introduction of the new 514 model, those who purchased this new car in various countries around the world sent letters to the factory, praising it unanimously. This proves that the new Vauxhall car truly outperforms others. For example, a person named Dennis, purchased a 514 two-seater new car from the Vauxhall branch in Madras, India. After trying it out, he was very satisfied and immediately wrote to the factory, describing his experience with the car. He traveled 435 miles, all on highland roads, 7,500 feet above sea level. On average, he could travel 33 miles per gallon of gasoline, which is equivalent to 8.5 liters of fuel per kilometer. This level of economy is unparalleled by other cars. In addition, the Milan Vauxhall factory also received a letter from Mr. Rocigande, the secretary of the International Automobile Exhibition, expressing his praise for the new Vauxhall car. His letter is as follows:

"I am writing to your factory in the hope that you will know my sincere admiration for the new Vauxhall car. In short, the Vauxhall car is definitely the finest car among small cars, which is truly a source of pride. In two months, I drove the new Vauxhall car for 9,000 kilometers, or 5,600 miles, using various speeds and driving on different roads. Whether high mountains or flat plains, I tested it thoroughly. As a result, there were never any problems along the way, and there were no stops for repairs. The engine was consistently smooth and exceptionally fast, which was very satisfying. As for gasoline consumption, it was also very economical. Seven and a half gallons of gasoline could travel a total of 186 miles." The performance of the new car can be imagined.

The Vauxhall's produced vehicles are not only the 514 model, which can economize on gasoline, but also other new cars. The Vauxhall's recent business policy focuses entirely on improving its products, reducing car prices, and allowing car owners to save on all costs. Even six-cylinder cars are no exception. For example, a person named Patterson in India purchased a six-cylinder Vauxhall 521C convertible. After driving it, he was very satisfied and told people that when he bought the car, the car dealer told him that each gallon of gasoline could guarantee 18 to 20 miles. Afterwards, after driving it, it was more than that, as each gallon could travel 24.8 miles. Recently, the factory also told customers that if anyone found the Vauxhall car to be less economical than other cars, they could write a letter explaining the reason. After the factory receives the letter, it can find ways to improve the shortcomings. This shows the Vauxhall's concern for economic issues.

Advertising Competition in the United States Automotive Industry

— Yan Yu

Today, the application of advertising techniques in the world is extremely valued by general merchants. In commercial competition, they rely on advertising as the sole weapon. Therefore, various commercial advertisements are also changing with each passing day, with endless variations. This phenomenon is particularly evident in the American automotive industry. In recent years, American automobile manufacturers have sprung up like mushrooms and flourished for a time, holding the hegemony of the global automobile industry. The fierce advertising competition among them is truly shocking to hear.

Generally speaking, advertisements from automobile manufacturers are published in every issue of American newspapers and magazines, filling up many pages. Several famous newspaper offices, such as the New York Times, the Chicago Tribune, and the Chicago Daily News, consider the annual automobile advertising revenue a significant income. It is said that the New York Times received more than US$5,500,000 in automobile advertising revenue last year, and the Chicago Daily News also had around US$300,000. Each manufacturer competes fiercely for the most advantageous automobile advertising position in newspapers, often making the editors of the newspapers find it difficult to decide. Because offending any party, if a break occurs, and the manufacturer stops sending advertisements, will greatly affect the newspaper's income. As for magazines, in addition to various automobile magazines, other magazines such as the nationally best-selling Saturday Evening Post, publish colorful automobile advertisements that are particularly vibrant and moving, greatly arousing people's desire to buy and achieving significant results.

In addition, the effectiveness of posters on the market is no less than that of newspapers and magazines. Even in remote rural villages, automobile advertisements of various colors are everywhere. The texts and pictures are mostly exceptionally vivid and interesting, often causing pedestrians to stop and watch unconsciously, leaving a deep impression in their minds. These posters vary in size and are mostly printed in color, often by famous advertising writers. Although the cost is quite high, they don't mind.

The use of electrical advertising has become increasingly common recently. Broadway in New York has always been known as the "City That Never Sleeps," with its richness and prosperity surpassing the entire city. It is especially lively at night, with traffic like a dragon and horses like water, as if it were daytime. Previously, only Ford had a magnificent electrical advertisement there, with bright and brilliant light that caught the eye of passersby. Now, Dodge, Austin, General Motors, and other manufacturers are unwilling to be outdone and have followed suit. For a time, it became fashionable to spend heavily to rent advertising space nearby and broadcast the latest electrical advertisements, with red and green lights reflecting each other, emitting ten thousand rays of light, even eclipsing the stars and moon.

Last spring, Ford came up with a unique idea and specially filmed the process of automobile manufacturing and all the scenes inside the factory, and showed these films free of charge at public institutions in major cities around the world. This film was brought to Shanghai this year and shown at places such as the University of Shanghai. Everything filmed in the film was exceptionally clear, from the purchase of raw materials to the completion of a car leaving the factory, all the procedures in between were filmed one by one. During the screening, the company also sent personnel to the scene to add a detailed explanation while the film was running. The film consisted of six reels and lasted one hour. At the same time, the company's employees also brought a large number of finely printed commemorative brochures and advertising leaflets, which were distributed to the audience on the spot as an aid to promotion.

General Motors is fond of social activities and specializes in planning all kinds of gatherings and competitions that are of interest to the public. For example, beauty contests for women are held in various bustling cities, and products from their factory are used as trophies to be awarded to the first-place winners. In addition, the factory often gives its latest products to social celebrities in various countries around the world to establish connections and promote publicity. This is indeed a new path in advertising techniques, with remarkably effective results that cannot be taken lightly.

Austin has recently introduced a car-giving program with a simple procedure. Anyone who can introduce ten customers to purchase the factory's automobiles will be given the latest model of a small sports car, priced at more than US$700. This method has been in effect for three months. Although car salesmen are complaining incessantly, the sales of the factory's products have indeed made surprising progress. This is also a good method in advertising competition.

News from Abroad

Automotive News from Abroad

— Song Yu

Flyer Car Wins Championship. Athens, Greece News. The Flyer car won a glorious victory in the Mount Parnassus hill climb race. This competition combines climbing speed into one, and the route is vast and long. In the seven and a half mile route, it rises 3,900 feet above sea level from the flat ground. The route almost reaches the top of the mountain and stops. The car nationality participating in the competition is broad and the types are also numerous, and the time is June 21st. In the second level of the competition, the first and second prizes were won by Flyer No. 514. The winner in the third level was the new model No. 522. All are enough to give Flyer a chance to show its climbing performance in Greece.

Buick Factory Increases Car Production. The Buick Motor Company in Flint, Michigan, USA, produced 18% more in March than in the same period last year. A total of 8,696 cars were produced in the factory in March 1930. In March 1931, its output increased to 10,271 vehicles. Therefore, the factory's activities increased by 32% compared to the same period last year.

Africa Builds Automobile Roads. The hinterland of Africa is sparsely populated. Those who arrive are only hunters and ivory merchants. Modern automobile roads have now been built. Items are transported by automobiles, so that nations that have not been in contact with the world can also slightly enjoy the tide of world evolution. After the new road is built, the industrial output can be expected in the near future. The car road between Minluo and Congo has been built. The 600-mile road from Alexandria to Luxor has also been successfully planned. Another road will be built to Timbuktu.

Chevrolet Will Reach 8 Million. According to the Chevrolet Motor Company officials, Chevrolet cars will soon reach 8 million. The time will be in the middle of this year. It also said that more than half of its company's products have been produced in the last four years.

Italian Lancia Freight Car (Manager of Pa Teh Wah Company)

News

Domestically Produced Heavy-Duty Truck

— Wu Fei

We have long been eager for domestic factories to manufacture automobiles to rival imported goods. Because in the past two decades, the automobile industry has become increasingly developed, and because the Chinese people cannot manufacture them themselves, all kinds of vehicles have to be purchased from Europe and the United States. The outflow of money has been difficult to record. Moreover, European and American countries regard the Far East as the only sales market for automobiles. Then the development of land and water transportation in China has become an opportunity for these countries to sell more cars, and there is no domestic car to come out. The lack of progress in material aspects is embarrassing. Recently, I read a Reuters report from Fanyang on June 19, stating that after the first domestically produced heavy-duty truck in China was completed, the Liaoning Arsenal held a celebration to commemorate the grand event. Factory Director Li Jun plans to send the car to various parts of North China for trial operation to promote publicity, etc. I cannot help but be delighted because the first domestically produced heavy-duty truck has been completed and opened a new era in the Chinese automobile industry. However, the manufacturing and process of the heavy-duty truck is not known in detail due to the brevity of the telegram. Recently, I read a description of the first domestically produced heavy-duty truck in the Beijing Morning Post. The matter is quite interesting. It said that three years ago, after the civil war ended, people in Liaoning said that Liao had two major arsenals and produced too much military equipment. They all wanted to use the factory's machines to make more useful tools. This idea was adopted by Zhang Xueliang, the authority of Northeast China. Therefore, the two factories were reorganized into factories. The Fanyang Arsenal is engaged in steel manufacturing, and produces a lot. Not only for the railway, but also has a huge sales market in China. The other factory, director Li Yijun, is engaged in fundamental and great work. He suggested that the factory should manufacture heavy-duty trucks to meet domestic needs, and said that the Chinese people all want to sit in cars. I will make the Chinese people understand the manufacturing method of cars so that they can sit and wait and get some comfort so that they do not often use foreign goods. Zhang Xueliang and other important officials in Northeast China agreed and gave him 750,000 yuan as start-up funds. Thus, work began. A Liaoning Arsenal Industrial Manufacturing Department was established, and the famous American automobile designer Maya was hired. He also contacted foreign automobile companies in order to purchase machines that he could not manufacture himself. After two years, the first car has recently been completed. The following description of manufacturing is worth noting: "Two types of heavy-duty trucks have been completed, one is McdIe75o and the other is McdIeIoo, specially prepared for Chinese demand, that is, specially prepared for walking on bad roads. Therefore, the speed is slower, and the vehicle is larger than any foreign-made car. The various details of the McpIe75 car chassis weigh 3,500 pounds. The body weighs 1,000 pounds. Excluding the weight of 4,000 pounds, the total weight is 8,500 pounds. The power is 615 horsepower. The normal speed is 25 miles per hour. The fastest speed is 44 miles per hour. The wheel is 142 inches high and the body is 9 feet long. The price is 1,070 gold yuan. The McdIeIoo car chassis weighs 4,600 pounds. The body weighs 1,400 pounds. Excluding the weight of 6,000 pounds, the total weight is 12,000 pounds. The power is 86 horsepower. The normal speed is 20 miles per hour. The fastest speed is 30 miles per hour. The wheel is 160 inches high. The body is 11 feet long. The price is 2,000 gold yuan. The following parts were purchased from foreign countries. (1) Engine. (2) Tires. (3) Electrical supplies. In addition, all the items used in the car are manufactured by the factory. Regarding purchases from foreign countries, Director Li said that foreign car manufacturers also do not manufacture all the car supplies in their own country. They also have to order from other countries. Because China currently does not have all kinds of application materials, it has to buy from foreign countries. He also said that he will strive for progress in the future. As mentioned above, Mcdle75o has been completed and tested. It is quite satisfactory, etc." From this description, the description of the domestically produced heavy-duty truck is detailed and thorough. In China, where industry is declining, there are actually domestically produced heavy-duty trucks. No wonder foreign telegrams are widely reported in Western newspapers. However, I still have something to say, that is, this first domestically produced car is specially designed for walking on bad roads. If it can be promoted and expanded, and the production of automobiles continues, it will be able to meet the needs of the Chinese people. Although, the Minsheng Factory affiliated to the Fanyang Engineering Corps has successfully built a new car. This is the first car made in China. I think that not only will the Liao Factory continue to manufacture to improve the quality and expand the application of the products, but factories across the country will also follow suit and increase day by day. This is indeed a cause for celebration for the future of China's industry. It also means a lot of recovery for the rights and interests.

Recent Situation of Road Construction in Various Counties of Guangdong

— Jun Chao

Dongguan. The streets of Dongguan County are narrow and traffic is very inconvenient. Recently, as various counties have started constructing automobile roads one after another, the magistrate of Dongguan County is determined to start constructing automobile roads to facilitate transportation. The County Public Works Bureau has completed the measurement of the automobile roads to be constructed and drawn the drawings. The first phase of the planned automobile roads is the lower market street, Maixian Street, Jiangu Street, Tieguo Street, and Maimu Street. The route of Maimu Street leads directly to the West Gate and connects with the Wanlongtai Highway. The route of the lower market street leads directly to the provincial city pier. The city wall will also be demolished and rebuilt into a ring road. The Construction Department has approved it, and construction will begin soon.

Jiujiang. The construction of automobile roads in Jiujiang City has been going on for many days. The first section starts from Guanglongdian in Xingfuli and ends at Dafudian in Xingrenli. It has now been built to Shibuli, about 600 feet long. Sidewalks on both sides have also been built for 500 feet. The entire project will be completed in about fifteen days. The second section starts from Sangxu Caiting Street and ends at the first gun tower. The paving of the road surface is underway, and the sidewalks on both sides have also been built for more than 100 feet. The third and fourth sections are being tendered. All the street stones are being dug up. The road bridge in front of the Municipal Bureau has been completed.

Southwest. The third phase of automobile roads in the southwest is now under construction. The route runs from Hebang to Taiping Street as one section, and from Tongrong Street to Mingjia Ancestral Hall as another section. The area width of both roads is 30 feet. The height of the filling depends on the unevenness of the original streets. Therefore, the Taiping Street section needs to be filled to a height of 12 feet, and the Mingjia Ancestral Hall section needs to be filled to a height of 6 feet. The shops along the route have moved to San Gong Temple and Gao Street for temporary business. The road project was originally scheduled to be completed in three months. However, the recent floods in the west have been slightly delayed and may not be completed on schedule.

Foshan. The Lanshi automobile road previously built in Foshan has now been completed and officially opened to traffic. There are many passengers. The public bus is operated by Lianhua Motor Company. For the convenience of passengers, new vehicles have been added to the service. The entire journey takes only 20 minutes. The entire route of the Funing automobile road has also been planned and will soon be tendered out for construction.

Chencun. The Chencun road construction project was originally divided into three lines, A, B, and C. The A line road has been surveyed and completed. The width was originally set at 30 feet. Recently, merchants along the road felt that the width was not suitable and jointly submitted a request to the Construction Department to construct the road according to the original plan of 50 feet wide. The Construction Department has considered the issue and found that the width of 50 feet on Nan'an and Tongle Streets is not a problem. However, the widest part of the main street can only be 34 feet. The road connects Nan'an Street, Tongle Street, and the main street. Construction will begin within days.

Social News

Foch's War Diaries (to be continued)

— Translated by Gu Angruo

Two days later, on July 23, I reiterated the previous order as follows: ... If our army is to achieve complete victory in this battle, the important key is to strike the enemy without delay. All strength should be fully supplied to the Tenth Army. The Tenth Army should concentrate these strengths on one part of its front line in order to carry out a powerful offensive in a particularly important area, namely the Datuna area. The Sixth Army assisted on the right, and the remaining forces were concentrated on the left wing. This attack threatened the enemy to withdraw from the entire area south of Datuna in a difficult state.

With all strength transferred to assist the Tenth Army, the Fifth Army will inevitably have only limited troops at its disposal. Therefore, the Fifth Army must implement chain warfare. Every battle must concentrate all its strength and create an advantage to prepare for the next battle. For example, progress towards the highlands north of the Anker River must create opportunities to facilitate an attack on the south side of the river. An attack on the south side of the river must threaten the enemy to withdraw from the area north of the Marna River.

At the time of this command and intensified fighting, I cannot ignore the possibility of a flanking attack by the German army in other directions. In order to escape our army's large encirclement, the Supreme Command of the Central European Empire may use its reserve troops north of the Coriasis River to attack the British line to hold it in check. I therefore asked Commander Petain to reassemble all the tired soldiers who had withdrawn from the front line behind the left wing of the French army to prepare. I also transferred the two British divisions that had been sent to the south of the Sham River on July 12 back to the command of General Haig.

The troops of the Sixth and Tenth Armies were mostly concentrated on both sides of the Orque River, and began to attack Orsy on July 25. In one great victory, Orsy was occupied. The eastern slope of Sherman Mountain, which controlled the Orque River basin, became a foothold for our army. This battle dispelled the enemy's hope of holding the Orque River defense line and became an important victory for our army.

The next day, the German army retreated to the highlands north of the river. The retreat was so rapid that our army's advance troops could not catch up.

On the evening of the 29th, the French Tenth, Sixth, and Fifth Armies stopped along the front of the Gran-le-Sour, Datuna, Circhi, Renny line on the highlands.

The enemy insisted on resisting stubbornly here. On July 30 and 31, our army wanted to defeat him, but it was in vain. The villages of Seringi, Serchi, and Felleraron were gained and lost several times. The war was in a stalemate.

According to my command on July 25 and Commander Petain's instructions on July 29, the Tenth Army attacked again at 4:45 a.m. on August 1. The French 25th, 41st, and 68th Divisions and the British 34th Division, with the assistance of tank artillery, charged the Granle Sour heights. Although the enemy resisted very fiercely, our army finally occupied the German line between Granle Sour, Sevenni, and Climaie with hand-to-hand combat. This decisive battle threatened the German army to retreat again.

At dawn on August 2, the Tenth, Sixth, and Fifth Armies saw that the enemy had retreated completely. The three armies did not fold up their troops and did not fire a single bullet until the evening, advancing to the highlands south of the Vance River. Shaason was thus recovered.

The progress continued on the 3rd, our army reached the left bank of the Vance River and made contact with the enemy again, with outposts crossing the river in several places.

On the 4th, our army encountered the German army defending the Vance River and had no intention of giving up. Our army must deploy a new offensive and transfer new strength lines to have hope of defeating the enemy. Even so, it is difficult to expect an immediate victory. Moreover, at this time, our army is preparing for another important battle, namely the Battle of Picardy and Santer. Our army's current number does not allow our army to undertake this battle and simultaneously launch an offensive against the Vance River. Therefore, I ordered the Central Reserve "to feign strength on the defense line south of the Vance River, so that the enemy would get the impression that our army was still preparing for a fierce attack."

In this way, after three weeks of fighting, the Second Battle of the Marne ended. The German army lost the battle on July 15, and the Allied forces launched a large-scale counter-offensive on the 18th, winning every battle. To this day, they still have the upper hand. The teams participating in the war included American, British, Italian, and French armies. The results of the war were quite important. The Allied forces captured 30,000 prisoners, more than 600 artillery pieces, and 3,000 machine guns. The front line was shortened by 28 miles, the Paris Sheron railway line was restored to traffic, and the danger in Paris was eliminated.

The German army's morale was dispersed, and our army's military appearance was greatly enhanced. Our army had previously been forced to take a defensive posture for four months due to the enemy's numerical superiority. Now, taking the opportunity to strike first, it has taken the initiative of the counter-offensive and leaped back to hold the lead in this long war. It is necessary to quickly mobilize the entire strength of the Allied forces and take advantage of the victory to wipe out the enemy before they recover their strength. (To be continued)
